To the Ten Directions and the Boundless World,
The **Elevating Life True Scrolls** are proclaimed below:
High Functionary [某] respectfully seals.
To the Southern Realm of the Vermilion Celestial World,
The **Precepts and Ritual Formulas** follow the old edition,
Respectfully, according to the scripture’s teachings,
The following doctrines have yet to be fully comprehended.

Now, taking from the *Nine True Wondrous Precepts Sutra*,
We adopt a revised and authenticated format,
So that the living may seek and transmit for the departed:
The **Supreme Precepts of the Nine True Wondrous Degrees**,
The **Golden Tablets of the Nine True Wondrous Degrees**,
And the **Elevating Life True Scrolls of the Southern Pole’s Longevity**.
Respectfully, according to the *Supreme Sovereign of the Primordial Origin’s Sutra on Extracting Offenses from the Nine Abysses*,
It states that when a person’s lifespan is exhausted,
They should enter the Nine Abysses,
Where the Black Register records their name,
And there is no means of liberation.

If there are spouses, sons, daughters, or fellow disciples of the same household,
Who establish a **Dao/Way Assembly** for the departed,
And request the transmission of the Nine True Wondrous Precepts,
While solemnly proclaiming the **Golden Tablets and White Scrolls of Elevating Life**,
And informing the Earthly Sovereigns,
Burning away the Black Register,
Then all the departed who are thus summoned
Shall be liberated in due time,
Their souls ascending to the Southern Celestial Court,
And through karmic connections,
They may attain the rank of **Nine True Wondrous Persons**.

Now, High Functionary [某] respectfully submits,
That the household of [某] devoutly practices the Dao,
Has constructed a Dao/Way Assembly at [某],
And requests the transmission of the Nine True Wondrous Precepts
For the departed recommended by [某].
The **Golden Tablets, White Scrolls, and Savior of Suffering Elevating Life True Scrolls** are hereby given.
You should attentively listen,
And meditate upon them in your mind.
In future lifetimes, when you are reborn among mortals,
Hold them as treasures of your body.

At that time, the **Supreme Sovereign of the Primordial Origin** shall proclaim the precepts,
Which are set forth below:

1. **Respect and yield** to others, **filially honor** parents;
2. **Diligently restrain** yourself, **loyally serve** the ruler;
3. **Do not kill**, **compassionately save** all beings;
4. **Do not lust**, **keep your body pure** and act righteously;
5. **Do not steal**, **extend virtue** and sacrifice for others;
6. **Do not be wrathful**, **do not harm** others with fierce anger;
7. **Do not deceive**, **do not flatter or harm** others with falsehoods;
8. **Do not be arrogant**, **do not scorn** the Supreme Truth;
9. **Do not waver**, **devoutly uphold** the precepts with singular dedication.

The **Precepts and Ritual Formulas** are as above.
The **Wondrous Precepts and True Scrolls** carry the most solemn prohibitions.
Now, according to the ritual, we issue the **Precepts and Ritual Formulas** to the departed [某].

After receiving and wearing them,
If one practices according to the Law,
There shall be **Inspecting Lifespan Children** and **Protective Precept-Wielding Deities**,
Who will guard and shield them as they meditate.

Those who receive the precepts
Should firmly uphold righteous mindfulness,
Forever severing evil roots,
Accumulating good deeds and merits,
To ultimately attain transcendence and realization.

Respectfully issued,
Year [某] Month [某] Day [某]

The **Transmitting Master of High Merit** [高功衔], **Precept Tablets of Skin and Surface** [戒牒皮面], **Transmitting Master** [姓名], **respectfully sealed** [谨封], **Precept Tablets of Skin and Back** [戒牒皮背]:

*"The Supreme Gold Seal for Transmitting Lifespan and the Nine True Wondrous Precepts"* [太上金箓度命九真妙戒], **given to the departed certain** [付亡人某] **to wear and receive**.

In ancient rites, simplicity was valued yet profound;
In modern times, the preference is for novelty and excess.
The **Precept Regulations** established by **Master Lü** [吕氏所校定制集],
when examined against the **Grand Treasury** [大藏],
and cross-referenced with the **scriptural rites** [经科],
show slight **obstructions** [窒碍];
one should not **lightly adopt** [轻取] them.

If one were to **relocate and transmit** [迁拔传度] the Precepts,
the ancients only used the **Nine True Precept Tablets** [九真戒牒] and the **Gold Seal with White Tablets** [金箓白简],
as recorded in the *"Sutra of Drawing Sins from the Nine Abysses"* [《九幽拔罪经》],
which is clearly documented.

Later, **practitioners of the Law** [法士] created **Precious Edicts** [宝诰],
imitating the imperial **edicts and commands** [诰命] given by the court.
Their disciples claim that the **Law Officials** [法官] of old,
when **bestowed with rank and merit** [曾受职品],
had **functional efficacy** [救济有功],
thus they speak of **advancing in rank** [进爵加秩],
**relocating according to merit** [随品命迁],
**presenting edicts to the Supreme Truth** [捧诰朝真],
and **calculating merits for rewards** [计功酬赏].

**Master Pù** [朴庵] thus **temporarily followed** [姑亦从之],
**revising and supplementing** [删定一式，补於集中] the format,
with its **preliminary explanations** [讲议] clearly detailed in the earlier passages.

In recent times, there are further innovations:
**Mysterious Talismans for Ascending to Heaven** [生天妙箓符命],
**Official Certificates and Certifying Documents** [公据由凭],
and the like—
**excessively fabricated** [多端撰造],
**gradually losing their original authenticity** [渐失本真],
**pursuing gain and competing for titles** [趋利争名],
**however, they no longer consider cause and effect** [岂顾因果].

Even as with the **Nine Dragon Talismans** [九龙符命],
there are **many conflicting versions** [多本异同],
and none can be **clearly traced** [莫知所逮].

Moreover, the **Talismans for Breaking the Underworld** [破地狱符],
given to the departed,
**already having undergone posthumous rites** [已承追抽诣坛],
**confessing sins and invoking the Supreme Truth** [忏罪参真],
after receiving the precepts—
**this conflicts with proper doctrine** [於义未通].

Additionally, within the **Precept Tablets** [戒牒],
the first is listed as the **"Precept of the Primordial Truth"** [初真戒]:
**reverence and humility** [敬让], **filial piety toward parents** [孝养父母];
The second is the **"Precept of Mindful Truth"** [念真戒],
**which is also questionable** [云云].

According to the **scriptures** [经],
the first is **reverence and humility** [敬让], **filial piety toward parents** [孝养父母];
The second is **"restraining diligence"** [克勤],
**and so forth** [云云],
**all clearly recorded** [具载备矣].

The **"Precept of the Primordial Truth"** [初真戒] and the **"Precept of Mindful Truth"** [念真戒]
are **the rites established by Master Guǎngchéng** [广成先生],
**elucidating the scriptural intent** [发明经旨],
**awakening the dim and the bright** [启悟幽明],
**yet how can they be mixed with the Supreme Sovereign’s** [天尊] **Golden Mouth** [金口] **proclamations**,
**and thus **disrupt the teachings** [相紊教法]?

It is **proper to clarify** [当为讲明] and **inform those who inquire** [以告知者].
I fear that the **unlearned** [无识之徒] may **decorate falsehoods to mislead themselves** [饰非以自惑],
**and such deviations are hardly surprising** [亦何足怪哉].

**Bathing Talisman**
This talisman is inscribed in cinnabar and burned, then cast into the bathing basin. The Daoist assembly recites the **Eight Heavenly Great Brahman Scriptures** [八天大梵文] in unison, while the master silently intones the **Three Lights Incantation** [三光咒], gathers the **qi** [炁], and blows it into the bathing chamber. The ritual is then performed.

**The Supreme Lord’s True Bathing and Soul-Conducting Talisman** [太上沐浴度魂真符], from *The Upper Clarity’s Secret Method of Rescue and Conduction* [《上清济度秘法》]:

By the command of the Supreme Lord,
For the departed souls of the late **such-and-such**,
We bathe their bodies and purify their **virtue** [浴德],
Wash away their turbidness and restore clarity [浣浊流清],
Dispel the sins and offenses accumulated across lifetimes,
Cleanse the guilt and defilement of past existences,
So that their spirits may be pure—
Worthy to don official robes and attend court,
Wearing precepts and holding scriptures,
Ascending to the True and awakening to the Dao,
As decreed by this talisman.
**Conducted in accordance with this command.**
**Year, Month, Day**

**Yellow Talisman’s General Commentary** [黄箓都疏]:
According to the **Golden Talisman Ritual’s** [金箓仪] general commentary format, two classes are arranged, with the first class listing the signatures and their merits. Since the fast is already observed, how could one know all the merits? Now, the **High Functionary’s full signature** [高功全衔] is used, thus aligning with the ritual’s requirements.

**Daoist Statutes, Volume Five Complete**
**Daoist Statutes, Volume Six**

**Collected by the Western Shu Daoist Pu’an Lü Yuansu**
**Compiled and Proofread by Zhuling Zhenyin Xu Xing, Hu Xianglong**
**Preface**

The Statutes are complete in their grand purpose,
yet lacking in communal rituals.
Devoted Daoists who hold deep faith,
discontent with the absence of authoritative texts for verification,
have entreated that future collections supplement what is missing.
Thus, to fulfill the Master’s intent—
which cannot be declined—
I have added further reference to complete the whole work.
Where discrepancies remain, I humbly submit them below,
awaiting the judgment of the learned.

---

**Ritual Offerings (Zhai)**
Master Guangcheng said:
There are twenty-seven grades of ritual offerings,
all detailed in the Three Caverns Scriptures,
each with its designated title and presiding deity.
What follows is the Left Path’s established practice.

**Taiyi Ritual (太一斋):**
Presided by the Ten Gods of Taiyi.
Emperors perform it to match celestial rites,
extending homage to Heaven.

**Jiutian Ritual (九天斋):**
Presided by the Nine Heavenly Birth Gods of the Emperor.
It rectifies the nation, safeguarding the dynasty and prolonging the age.

**Jinquan Ritual (金箓斋):**
Presided by the Upper Primordial Heavenly Official.
It protects the emperor, secures the people, and pacifies the land.

**Yujuan Ritual (玉箓斋):**
Presided by the Middle Primordial Earthly Official.
It protects the Six Palaces, aids the empress and consorts—
thus, it is the emperor’s ritual.
Or, for high officials and regional governors,
when praying for the nation’s safety,
its observance is also permitted.

**Huangquan Ritual (黄箓斋):**
Presided by the Lower Primordial Waterly Official,
concerning the Upper and Middle Primordial Palaces.
It universally benefits the family and state,
saves the living and the dead,
opens the path for the Seven Ancestors,
and rescues those in the Three Realms of Suffering.

**Mengzhen Ritual (盟真斋):**
For relocating ancestral temples or rescuing the deceased,
and for officials rescuing the lost—
all may be observed in conjunction.

**Dongyuan Ritual (洞渊斋):**
Presided by the Northern Emperor.
It dispels epidemics and sweeps away malevolent qi.

**Jiuyou Ritual (九幽斋):**
It kindles lamps to dispel darkness,
and rescues lost souls.

**Wulian Ritual (五炼斋):**
For Daoists in practice who set up rites for the departed.
It transmigrates spirits, calms the soul, and expiates sins.

**Zhengyi Ritual (正一斋):**
For transmitting scriptures and talismans,
and conferring the Dao.
It transmits the numinous and talismans,
upholds orthodoxy, and eliminates heresy.

The above ten ritual grades all have prescribed rites.
The remaining seventeen grades are detailed in Master Guangcheng’s
*Huangquan Sequence of Ritual Matters*,
though some may have titles without complete rites.

Additionally, there are the **Fifty Altars of the River Diagram Rituals (河图众醮)**,
each with established rites by Master Guangcheng,
created as needed—
yet few in the world know them,
and only a few are commonly observed.
Other regulations are fully recorded in the Daoist Canon,
primarily comprising expiatory methods.

**River Diagram Inner Canon: Three Palaces’ Stellar Expiation Ritual (河图内篇三宫辰曜解禳星运醮):**
Presided by the **Eleven Stellar Deities (十一曜)**.
It expiates calamitous stellar influences,
brings blessings, and prolongs life.

**River Diagram Primordial Records: Southern and Northern Twin Ministries’ Longevity Ritual (河图元纪南北二司延生同醮):**
Concerning the **Southern and Northern Dipper Stars (南北斗)**.
It prolongs life and reduces death,
heals illness, and dispels misfortune.

**Xuanling Northern Dipper Seven Elements Longevity Ritual (玄灵北斗七元延生醮):**
Exclusively venerating the **Seven Elements (七元)**.
All prayers made here shall be answered.

**Nine Dragons Rain-Invoking Ritual (祈雨九龙醮) & Rain-and-Snow Invocation Ritual (祈求雨雪醮):**
For the sake of the nation and its people,
to summon rain and snow.

**Five Emperors’ Pacification Ritual (五帝安宅醮):**
It secures the dwelling, repels crimes,
and pacifies spirits while warding off malevolence.

**Zitang Northern Obscurity Ritual (紫庭北阴醮):**
Exclusively venerating the **Northern Dipper (北斗)**.
For deep calamities and grave afflictions,
where prayers seem unanswered;
when malevolent spirits haunt the home,
causing depletion and loss;
when official advancement stalls,
or unjust grievances remain unresolved—
after three such rituals,
extraordinary responses shall be attained.

**Riverhead Substitution and Severance Ritual (河头代命断除复连水醮):**
For successive years of calamity,
premature deaths of descendants,
ghostly oppressions,
or the deceased returning to haunt the living—
first, the Chapter Ritual is performed to preserve and rescue the lost.
Upon completion, **fourteen individuals** substitute their forms for ten objects in a solemn oath,
and a boat is prepared by the river to dispatch the severed influences—
hence, it is called the **Riverhead Ritual**.

**Disaster Expiation and Merit Augmentation Ritual (消灾益算醮):**
Petitions are submitted to seek mercy,
and expiatory prayers are offered.

**Zhengyi Transmission Ritual (正一传度醮):**
For receiving talismans and scriptures,
and protecting both men and women.

The above are all rites established by Master Guangcheng.

**Reserved Blessing and Fate-Fixing Ritual (储福定命醮):**
Presided by the **Nine Heavenly Elders (九天丈人)**.
It is performed on one’s birthday.
The Venerable Elders expound the *Opening of Heaven Scripture*,
stating that on one’s birthday,
one should reflect on the preciousness of life
and repay one’s parents’恩.
This ritual also teaches principles of self-preservation and bodily care.

**Replacement and Extension of Life Ritual (更籍换按续命延生醮):**
Venerating the **East Peak (东岳)** and the **Seventy-Two Directors (七十二司主)**.
For those in critical illness or grave affliction,
one may receive the **Five Precepts (五戒)**,
abandon past misdeeds, and seek renewal,
striving earnestly for divine response.

**East Peak Longevity Ritual (东岳延生醮):**
Exclusively venerating the **Yule Sovereign (岳皇)**.
It prolongs life and expiates sins.

**Northern Pole True Martial Ritual (北极真武醮):**
Exclusively venerating **True Martial (真武)**.
It invites blessings and dispels malevolence.

The above are all rites established by **Weixian Chao Gong (尉仙巢公观)**.

**Wenchang Fortune-Invoking Ritual (文昌祈禄醮):**
For praying to **Wenchang (文昌)** to attain official rank and blessings.

**Auspicious Invocation and Lineage Preservation Ritual (祈祥保嗣醮):**
The *Scripture for Guiding Beings (度人经)*, Volume 4, contains the *Scripture for Invoking Descendants (祈嗣经)*.
It prays for the preservation of lineage and the unblocking of blessings.

**Six Jia Fetal Protection Ritual (六甲保胎醮):**
The *Scripture for Guiding Beings*, Volume 36, contains the *Scripture for Protecting the Fetus (保胎经)*.
The ritual invokes the **Six Jia and Sixty Spirit Generals (六甲六十神将)**,
protecting and nurturing the fetal essence to fulfillment.

**Zhengyi Tomb Pacification Ritual (正一安坟醮):**
It secures graves, repels crimes, and pacifies spirits.

**Oath-Fire Disaster Expiation Ritual (誓火禳灾醮):**
It thanks the **Mars Star (火星)** and expiates the *Backfire Calamity (回禄)*.

**Nine Obscurities Sin-Expiation Ritual (九幽拔罪醮):**
Presided by the **Nine Obscurities Penitential Law (九幽忏法)**.
It rescues the deceased and expiates sins through penance.

**Volitional Rebirth Ritual (随愿往生醮):**
Presided by the **Ten Directions’ Celestial Worthies and True Persons (十方天尊真人)**.

**Guiding the Departed to Volitional Rebirth**
To lead the deceased to rebirth as they wish.

**The Various Rituals Above**
When performed on a grand scale, they span successive nights and days; when moderate, they extend through day and night until completion. All may be adapted to circumstances, with petitions submitted to seek blessings and divine command. If one’s strength is insufficient to fulfill them fully, a single morning of Daoist practice may suffice.

**The Lingbao Cavernous Mysteries Natural Expiation for the Departed Ritual (灵宝洞玄自然拔亡醮)**
*With prescribed rites*
It clarifies the **Supreme Primordial Dao’s** intent, rescuing and expiating the departed souls.

**The Daoist Ascension and Transference Ritual (道士升化迁度醮)**
*With prescribed rites*
For the Daoist’s final ascension and the transfer of their spirit.

**The Shangqing Cultivation of the True and Expiation of Sins Ritual (上清修真谢罪醮)**
For Daoists cultivating the True, to dispel calamities and atone for sins.

**Master Guangcheng’s Teaching**
*"Ritual"* is but another name for sacrifice.
Incense, flowers, lamps, and candles—
Fruits, wine, tea, and offerings—
Summon the heavens and earth, gather the myriad spirits,
Expiate calamities and pray for blessings,
Benefiting all under heaven.

Its method originates from the *Scripture of the River Diagram’s Dragon Text on Primordial Transformation and Imperial Auspicious Divine Response (河图龙文元化帝瑞神经)*.
First, purity is essential; spirit is the foundation.
With sincere resolve and unwavering devotion, one seeks communion.
Whatever is petitioned or expiated—
Compose prayers and prostrations with precision,
Ensure the scriptures are authentic and the rites genuine,
Striving for solemn reverence.

Yet if performed carelessly, with reckless haste or deceit,
Defrauding the True and the Saints,
One invites only guilt and retribution—
How then can blessings be attained?

**Exhortation**
*Strive, strive.*

**Arranging the Ritual Platform’s Directions**
According to Master Guangcheng’s *Sanqi* (三箓) sequence,
The **Five Directions’ True Scriptures** are proclaimed on the night of platform establishment,
Placed upon the five directional altars,
Each sealed with a **Golden Dragon** to mark their order.
Thus, the directions are distinguished and aligned,
Awaiting the grand ritual’s completion,
When the True Scriptures are invoked and the incantations delivered,
Burning the petitions to ascend into the azure void—
This is the true framework of the ritual ground.

Indeed, during practice, **visualization is paramount**.
East, west, south, north—
Each must be held in mind,
Not to be forced or compromised.

There are those who delight in unconventional doctrines, claiming that wherever the **Celestial Sovereign** descends, it must face true north, regardless of the hall’s orientation—always placing the **Imperial Seat** as the northern direction. A single misguided thought thus reverses the positions of heaven, earth, and the four quarters—this is far from orthodox reasoning and must not be followed.

**On Arranging the Ritual Chapters**
I observe that ritual chapters are often rigidly tied to a specific day. If a palace, temple, or private residence has spacious halls with secluded grounds suitable for the designated day, one may purify the mind and proceed accordingly. Otherwise, the clamor of bells and drums, the comings and goings within and without, will disrupt the ritual, leaving the practitioner’s mind unsettled. How then can one avoid errors, omissions, or grave mistakes? Often, this leads to profound blunders. When pressed for time and unable to adjust, the **Ritual Master** will surely be displeased—this is most harmful.

If the ritual chapters contain no hidden or secret matters, they should be written, reviewed, and sealed in advance during a quiet day, leaving only the **Taoist Pure Script** to be inscribed on the appointed day. This ensures no mistakes, which is entirely proper. Even if minor deviations from the prescribed texts arise, one must adapt pragmatically—this is far better than rigid adherence leading to gross error.

**On Sealing the Ritual Chapters**
When the **High Functionary** seals the chapters, the transmitted **Book-Symbol** above is called the **"Opening of the Celestial Gate Symbol."** Upon examination, this is incorrect. The **Symbol** originates from the *Six Jia* (六甲) scriptures and is called the **"Yin-Yang Symbol."** For instance, *Jiazi* (甲子) belongs to **Yang**, and its **Symbol** is the **Standing Blade**. *Yibao* (乙丑) belongs to **Yin**, and its **Symbol** is the **Three-Lined Mark**. It also appears in the *True Martial Three-Array Method* scriptures, likewise divided into **Yin-Yang**. There is also the **Dispersed-Form Incantation**, and the current **Three-Lined Mark** is the **Yin Symbol**. Once the chapters are delivered to heaven, a **Yang Symbol** must be used—this distinction must not be overlooked. Now recorded in this text for all to understand.

**Yang Symbol (Dispersed Form)**
**Yang Symbol (Concentrated Form)**
**Yin Symbol (Concentrated Form)**

「Midheaven Great Sage [1]
   Swift as the Flying Heaven,
   Seizing the **Yang Jade** [2]—**Jade Boundary** [3]—of the Five Regions,
   Capturing the **Ghosts of No Dao/Way** [4] and delivering them to the **First Northern Prison** [5],
   Punishing them according to the law.
   Tang Ge Zhou, the Third General,
   **True Martial General** [6] **Standing Blade** [7] awaits,
   **Yin Symbol (Dispersed Form)** [8].

   Midheaven Great Sage [1]
   Swift as the Flying Heaven,
   Seizing the **Yin Jade** [2]—**Jade Boundary** [3]—of the Five Regions,
   Capturing the **Ghosts of No Dao/Way** [4] and delivering them to the **First Northern Prison** [5],
   Punishing them according to the law.
   Tang Ge Zhou, the Third General,
   **Imperial Decree of the Three Officials of Heaven, Earth, and Water** [9],
   **Green Script** [10].

   During the Tang Dynasty’s **Tianbao Era** [11], the decree was issued to the **Officials of the Supreme Clarity Palace** [12],
   All donned **coronation robes** [13], halted the **Sacrificial Tablet** [14], and changed it to the **Green Script** [10],
   Written upon paper.
   As seen in **Du You’s *Comprehensive Institutions*** [15], the Tang Dynasty revered **Laozi** [16] as the **Holy Ancestor** [17],
   Established the **Supreme Clarity Palace** [12], and conducted rites of worship with utmost solemnity,
   Hence this decree was given.
   By the Song Dynasty, **Emperor Zhenzong** [18] further designated **Green Script** [10] as **Green Words** [19].
   The meaning of **Supreme Clarity** and **Green Words** [10] originates from distinct traditions.

   **Treasure Edict** [20]
   The **Treasure Edict** [20] comes from the **Sacred Scriptures** [21],
   Given to those who practice the Dao [22], bearing **rank and virtue/power** [23].
   After their **transformation and dissolution** [24], they are granted the **Treasure Edict** [20],
   Ascending in **stage and hierarchy** [25].
   Therefore, the final two **Symbols** [26] state:
   *“According to rank, command hierarchy; aligned with the divine, equal in status.”*
   *“Advance in **爵** [27] and add to **秩** [28]; follow rank, command promotion.”*
   Currently, these are uniformly applied, causing much confusion.
   If the deceased were not one who received the **Sacred Scriptures** [21], held **rank and virtue/power** [23],
   Or performed **meritorious deeds** [29], it is proper to omit the final two **Symbols** [26].

   **Scripture and Ritual Model by Chancellor Ouyang Xiu** [30]
   **Green Words for the Emperor’s Native Command Dao Field**

   In the year of **某号** [31], the **某甲子** [32] cycle,
   On the **某月** [33] of the **某朔** [34] day, **某甲子** [32],
   The subject of the **Sons of Heaven** [35], **某**,
   Humbly dispatches **某人** to **某州** [36]’s **某宫观** [37],
   To open and initiate the **Native Command Dao Field** [38],
   Observing three days and nights of **ceasing dispersion** [39],
   Establishing a **great expiatory ritual** [40] in one setting.
   **The following words are presented to the Supreme Lord, the Jade Emperor of the True and Containing Dao, who governs the Heavenly Realm and holds the **Symbols of Dao/Way** [41]:**

   With deepest reverence, the **Treasure of Destiny** [42] is boundless,
   The **Vast Sky** [43] bestows **auspicious blessings** [44].
   On this **auspicious day** [45], Your **ritual presence** [46] descends upon the **Original Command** [47],
   The **great expiatory ritual** [40] now commences under the **ancient rites** [48].
   With **sincere offerings** [49] and **devout supplications** [50],
   The **Sages of Truth** [51] are summoned, their **spiritual essence** [52] gathered together.
   We pray for Your **divine grace** [53] to spread,
   That You may **bestow blessings upon the humble and the departed** [54],
   So that **seasons align in harmony** [55],
   And **ranks and virtues/powers** [56] are balanced in **rest and tranquility** [57].
   There is no limit to our **earnest and heartfelt devotion** [58].

   **The following words are presented.**
   **The Emperor for the benefit of the late **Jin Guo** [59]’s wife, the Du family,**
   **To offer **sincere commendation** [60] and **rescue from the Nine Abysses** [61].**」

**Ritual Invocation**

Life is born yet must end—this is called the **constant of things** [62].
The **Dao/Way** is formless in its origin, yet truly relies upon **mysterious aid** [63].
With **pious reverence** [64], we depend upon the **celestial abode** [65],
And solemnly purify this **ritual site** [66].

We **pursue the departed’s virtue/power** [67], now distant,
And **hope for the luminous spirit’s** [68] gracious protection.

The **Nine Regions** [69] are vast, all beings dwell in their kinds.
Only the **river and mountain peaks** [70] house the **numinous** [71],
And bind the **true immortals** [72] as their **overall governance** [73].
We **revere the hidden Dao/Way’s** mysteries,
And **gather the pure texts** [74] of the **jade tablets** [75],—
Like the **scaled brilliance** [76] of golden dragons.

Now, for **suppression and pacification** [77],
We **invigorate with earnest sincerity** [78].

May Your **penetrating insight** [79] shine upon us,
And **pure blessings** [80] be bestowed with favor—
**Secure the eternal stability** [81] of the realm and its people,
And **harmonize all living things** [82] so they may thrive in peace.

The **ritual invocation’s** text is **succinct yet complete**;
The **earlier collection** [83] has already spoken in detail.
Now, I take **Master Ouyang’s** [84] three invocations and present them here,
So that they may be **revered as models** [85].

Moreover, the **Yellow Announcement** [86] invocations—
Whether for **three chants** [87] or **nine chants** [88]—
All **fail to encompass** the six realms:
**Household, departed, ghosts, and spirits** [89].

Recently, **Master Fan of the Two Rivers** [90] in the **Ritual Ministry** [91]
Set up a **grand offering** [92],
And **first adopted** the **Nine Times of Recitation** [93] as the basis for his work,
Composing **nine invocations** [94] to be **recited at each hour** [95],
**Perfectly conforming** to the **ritual protocols** [96].

Now, I take the **full texts of the Opening and Dispersing** [97] rituals,
**Engrave and circulate them**, and **annotate the passages drawn from Daoist scriptures** [98],
So that they may serve as **reference for those who seek the method** [99].

Those **from Confucian texts** [100]—
Let **scholars and officials** [101] know their source.

**Yellow Announcement Invocation**
**Opening the Ritual Platform** [102]

**Yellow Announcement Invocation**
**Opening the Ritual Platform**

The Daoist altar stands solemn and pure, its sacred herbs ascending in radiant effulgence.
The celestial wind carries the harmonious tones of the **Eight Assemblies** [97],
As the **Eight Assembly Scriptures** and **Nine-Point Cloud-Signature Scriptures** gather in splendor upon the **Five-Luminous Seat** [98].
The *Nine Abysses Scripture* speaks of the **Jade Seat in Clouds of Treasure**,
And the *Ascending to the Mysterious Scripture* describes the **Five-Luminous Palace**, where the **Extreme Emperor of the North** gazes upon the **Flowering Dao**.
Now, with reverent devotion, we open the ritual hall to offer sincerity.

The **Feathered Canopy and Jade Banners** descend in vibrant array,
While **Golden Script and Jade Characters** unfold boundless enlightenment.
Thus, we return the radiance of **Dao and Virtue**,
And humbly fulfill the hopes of **humans and the Celestial**.

**Prayer to the Sacred:**
Receiving the **Augmented Manifest Command**,
We proclaim the **True Symbols of the Supreme Sovereign**,
Ascending to the **Highest Vehicle**,
And attaining the **Sincere Devotion of the Seal-Bearer**.

May the **Boundless Benevolence** of the **Most Merciful** be ever deepened,
And the **Dreaming Age** of the **Sacred Ones** forever transcended.
Before the **Heavenly Blessings** are proclaimed,
May they endure as **Divine Masters** for eternity.

Nine thousand *li* span the land—
Collecting the merit of the **Four Seas**;
Threefold **Dragon-Shouts of Ten Thousand Years**—
No reckoning can measure the **Two Imperial Courts**.

In the **Highest** and **C孝宗 Imperial Courts**, the **Dao endures unbroken**,
And with **Heaven**, they abide eternally.
The *Scripture of Salvation* states:
*"Preserving the **Eon-Measure**, ensuring **Heaven’s perpetuity**."*

**For the State’s Boundary Rites—Warding Disasters:**
The **Dragon-Filet Scriptures** safeguard the **Eight Auspicious Symbols**,
As the *Scripture of Salvation* declares:
*"The **Red Script, Jade Characters, and Eight Auspicious Dragon-Filets** preserve the **Eon-Measure**, ensuring **Heaven’s perpetuity**."*

The **Phoenix Calendar** records the **Thousand-Year Statutes**,
While the **Nine Temples** proclaim blessings,
And the **Three Spirits** offer auspicious rites,
**Stemming the Six Extremes** before they manifest,
And **universally nurturing all beings** to fulfillment.

Let **Unity of Virtue** restore the **Ancient Winds of Governance**,
And in **Ten Thousand Years**, may all ascend to the **Imperial Polarity**.

**Heaven’s Calamities** shall be utterly dispelled,
And the **Radiance of Transformation** shall bloom eternally.

**For the State’s Boundary Rites—Divine Sacrifices:**
Ascending the platform to expound the **Teachings**,
We uphold the **Rites of Praying for Grain**,
As the **Aiding-Sage True Lord** declares:
*"The **Yellow Announcement Ritual** is for praying for grain and auspicious timing."*

For the **State’s Accumulation of Auspicious Omen**,
We earnestly cultivate the **Devotion of the Modest and Upright**.

Under **Heaven’s Cover**, no spirit remains unvenerated.
Having gathered before the **Luminous Ones**,
We must **Guide and Welcome** them to the **Sacrificial Feast**.

Endowed with **Imperial Blessings**,
Their **Virtue and Might** shall shine ever brighter.
Assisting the **Primordial Transformation** with **Mysterious Devotion**,
We safeguard the **Ten Thousand Realms** in **Joyous Tranquility**.

**For the Ritual of Transcendence and Elevation:**
As **Heaven is High and Earth Profound**,
We unite in **Sincere Gratitude to the Source**.
With **Thunderous Urgency and Windlike Speed**,
None surpass the **Haste of Salvation**.

The **Temporal Guest Rites** declare:
*"The **Dragon-Han Scriptures** emerged from **Great Possession**,
And the **Red Clarity** unfolded in the **Upper Purity**—
Thus, from the **Eon-Cycle’s beginning**, all have deemed **Salvation the Urgent Matter**."*
It is further said:
*"The merit of **Salvation is supreme**—
Fire and Wind shall not cease,
Nor shall **Paths, Mountains, and Rivers** delay the transmission."*

Lamenting the **Eternal Separation of Kith and Kin**,
The *Scripture of Salvation* states:
*"Across the **Eons**, kindred souls yearn for the **Shining Mirror’s** side."*

Compassionately relieving the **Sunken Wronged**,
We dissolve their **Entangled Litigations**,
As the *North Dipper Scripture* attests:
*"The **Sunken Litigations** are examined and extracted from the **Dew-Curve Treasury**,
And the *Scripture of Salvation* declares:
*'Entering the **Daoist Palace**, the **Land of Bliss**.'*
The *Chapter on Transcendence* states:
*'Entering the **Daoist Palace**, the **Land of Bliss**.'*

Abandoning **Illusion**, returning to **Truth**,
We forever sever the **Net of Delusion**,
As the *North Dipper Scripture* proclaims:
*"Exiting the **Paths of Delusion**, we revert to **Primordial Return**,
And ascend through the **Gates of All Marvels**."*
And the *Laozi* teaches:
*"The **Mysterious, yet more mysterious**—
The **Gate of All Marvels**."*

**For the Promotion and Elevation of the Earth and Water Officials to the Celestial Ranks—Petitioning the Removal of Living and Deceased Sins:**
The **Vast Daoist Realm** and the **Boundless Abyssal Treasury** govern the **Domain of Obscurity**,
Yet none have ascended to the **Court of Supreme Marvels**.
Relying on **Boundless Mercy**, we universally extend **Compassionate Aid**,
As the **Fetters of the Netherworld** dissolve in **Sweet Dew**,
And the **Gates of Darkness** brighten with **Celestial Radiance**.

The *Scripture of Rescue from Suffering* states:
*"The **Flaming Obscurity** becomes the **Pure Office**,
And the **Sword-Trees** transform into **Cypress Groves**."*
The *Scripture of Salvation* declares:
*"Floating upon the **Celestial Radiance**, we present the **Registers before the Emperor**,
And wash away the **Multitudes of Sins** of the **Four Existence**."*
The *Scripture of Salvation* further states:
*"Holding the **Announcement Tablets**, we align before the Emperor."*

Returning to the **Celestial Ranks**, we sing of the **Pure Joys of the Eight Extremes**.
The **Divine Journey** through the **Eight Extremes** forever frees us from the **Wheel of Suffering**,
And all attain the **Shores of the Dao**.

**For the Six Realms of Sentient Beings:**
Lost in the **Crossing’s Delusion**, they have not yet returned,
And the **Filthy Sea** knows no shore.
We invoke the **Flowing Light of the Sacred Ones**,
And with **Piercing Clarity**, we dispel the **Deepest Ignorance**.

Knowing their **Past Lives**,
As the *Nine Abysses Scripture* attests:
*"The **Heavenly Venerable**, with the **Six Perfections of Wisdom**, commands all guilty souls to close their eyes and reflect—
In a moment, they shall **know their past lives**, each clearly revealed."*

Instantly awakening to their **Original Heart**,
They are illuminated by the **Flowering Radiance of the Morning Star**,
As the *Chapter on the Living Spirit* states:
*"The **Suffering Souls** sink into the **Nine Nights**,
And at dawn, they yearn for the **Morning Star’s** ascent."*

Purifying their **Darkness of Night**,
They **Chew the Jade Sounds** to refine their **Spirit-Souls**,
And **Bathe in the Golden Elixir** to **Nurture the Divine**,
As the *Scripture of Salvation* states:
*"The **Jade Sounds** gather the **Qi**,"*
And the *Scripture of Purity* declares:
*"The **Golden Elixir** refines the **Form**."*

Escaping the **Nine Abysses**, they point toward the **Red Celestial Dao** to receive **Transformation**;
Soaring beyond the **Three Realms**, they clear the **Mysterious Path** to attain **Truth**.

The **Southern Red Celestial Dao** is the **Furnace of Salvation**,
Transcending the **Color Realms, Desire Realms, and Formless Realms**.

**For the Dissipation of Calamities:**
Even within the same household, **half a lifetime** may bring **endless hardship**.

「夫妇同诚」— When husband and wife unite in sincerity,
「陈往愆而自省」— they confess past transgressions and reflect upon themselves,
「托妙供以祈哀」— they offer sacred oblations to beseech compassion.

「释冤而万罪除」— Their karmic debts are absolved, and all offenses vanish;
「扶衰而九厄解」— they are sustained in decline, and the Nine Calamities are dispelled.
「导以延生之**Qi**」— Guided by the **Qi** of prolonged life,
「诱其为善之衷」— they are drawn toward the heart of virtue.

Their latent karmic burdens fade away,
No longer ensnared by the **Six Dusts**—
**Six Dusts**: form, color, scent, taste, contact, and **dharma**.

Worldly entanglements are swiftly resolved,
Ultimately resting in the **Great Possession’s** domain.
*The Scripture of Salvation*: **"Great Possession’s** wondrous abode."

Together with their deep emotions,
They forever return to the **Primordial Transformation**.

Repaying their parents’ toil and labor,
They serve the **Great Lady of the House** with filial devotion—
Laboring through countless **kalpas**,
Their gratitude is profound, yet the debt remains unpaid.

With one heart of joy and fear,
Their sorrow runs deep, yet is not yet resolved.
May they discern my plea from the **Middle of the Way**,
And open the boundless compassion of the **Supreme**.

Especially to save the departed and preserve the living,
That they may shun evil and follow virtue.

The **Azure Palace** bestows life—
*The Scripture of Salvation*: **"The Azure Palace of the Eastern Flower**,
From which issue the Nine Dragons’ precious command,
To rescue the Nine Abysses’ hidden **Jade Sounds** and revive the dead **Spirit-Souls**,
So that their past names may bear good fortune.
They are raised as **Daoist Transcendents**;
*The Scripture of Salvation*: **"**The **Daoist Transcendent** attains humanity, with **Azure Records** extending their years**."**
*The Ritual of Nesting*: **"The Red Platform records virtue, the Azure Records extend years."**

The **Azure Palace** grants eternal release from the dusty toils of existence.
May they further pray for the bestowal of blessings,
And spread the Dao’s grace to all sentient beings.

To proclaim the merits of the **Daoist Transcendents** and **Jade Sounds**,
They are recorded in the **Stern Law Assembly**,
And announced to the **Ten Thousand True Ones**—
All receive their singular merits,
And are universally embraced by the **Way**.

The **Ten Thousand Ranges** are subdued and restored,
*The Scripture of Salvation*: **"The Ten Thousand Ranges flourish and expand."**
The gathered **Spirit-Souls** gallop in swift obedience.
Their virtues multiply without bound,
And the **Manifested Deities**’ assistance is truly abundant.

It is fitting to proclaim great rewards,
First to the **Spirit Officials**,
And to this lineage of the **Illustrious Dao**,
Lest they be guilty of profaning the **Sacred**.

Together they offer **Confession and Repentance**,
And await the **Grace of Pardon** with reverence.
**Dispersing the Ritual Platform**—
In ancient rites, no words were spoken aloud for dispersal,
Only the silent invocation of the heart.
Later generations added them,
Yet still, the meaning was not fully conveyed.
At the **Opening of the Ritual Platform**,
To express the hope for the **Dao’s favor**,
Even this was somewhat unclear.
It is best to remain with the **Heart Words** alone.

The **Celestial Master’s** established rites follow this intent.
After the **Three Offerings**,
There are designated words for the **Leaping Banquet** to address the **Supreme True One**,
And if one wishes to use words,
They must conclude the **Three Offerings** first,
Then present the petition—**only this is permitted**.

The **Phoenix Chariot** departs in solemn procession,
And the **Ten Thousand Cavalry** return swiftly home;
*The Scripture of Salvation*: **"A hundred million cavalry, floating through the void, arrive."**

The **Dragon Relay** proclaims the merits,
And delivers **Tablets of Petition**—
Ascending the **Nine Heavens** in a straight line.
All within the **Three Realms** are granted
A single purifying grace.
They are bathed in the **Dao’s mysterious subtleties**,
And taste the **Jade Tablets** while soaring aloft.
The **Heart’s resolve** is fulfilled,
And tears of gratitude flow naturally.

The **Daoist Transcendents’** banners vanish into the clouds,
Their divine wanderings now distant;
Gazing upon the **Sky’s Hook** in the **Celestial Sovereign’s** abode,
Their dreams plunge into the void.

**Tablets to the Mystic Caverns**—
With the **Ritual of Fasting** fulfilled,
The **Heavenly Inspection** is clear and evident,
Yet still the **Five Elders’** talismans are proclaimed,
And the **Jade Tablet Incantation**,
The **Celestial Sovereign’s** **Five Elders’** **Red Scriptures** with **Golden Characters**,
Are sent to the **Ten Directions’** **Palaces**.

The **Golden Dragon’s** **Cloud Cavalry** race without pause,
And the **Fire-Wind** does not cease;
They knock upon the **Jewel Hall’s** **Rock Gate**,
Yet the **Smoke and Mist** do not hinder.

With solemn offerings and splendid recommendations,
Their sincerity is fully exhausted,
Hoping to attain the **Ten Thousand Blessings**,
And harmonize with the **Great Thousand** **Worlds**.

**Palace of the Earthly Sovereign**—
Praying for blessings from the **Celestial Sovereign**,
And receiving life from the **Central Palace**,
They reaffirm the **Golden Button’s** **White Faith’s** **pledge**,
And reveal the **Dragon Tablet’s** **Jade Scriptures** with **Red Characters** as secrets.

All **Deities** hear in unison,
*The Scripture of Salvation*: **"All Deities listen to the Nine Earths’ hidden responses."**
They absolve the **deeply buried** **Spirit-Souls**,
And erase the **Records of Sin**.

They further present the **Clear and Pure Petition**,
And send **Tablets** with names inscribed to the **Central Palace**,
Listing them in the **Clear and Pure Register**.
They ascend to the **Court of the Daoist Transcendents**.

**Palace of the Watery Sovereign**—
With **Jade Tablets** meticulously inscribed,
They proceed to the **Pearl Palace**,
Recognizing the **Yellow Arrow’s** **singular merits**,
And seeking the **Nine Heavens’** **pure audience**.

They gather all **Aspirations**,
And freely communicate with the **Ten Thousand Spirits**,
Uniting the **multitude** to awaken,
And joining the **Seven Mysteries** to attain deliverance.
The **River of Love** is exhausted,
And the **Sea of Law** remains ever pure.

The **Words of Lord Ouyang** in his petition to the **Jade Emperor’s** **Sacred Title**
Are the **actual facts** of our **Current Dynasty**,
Later confirmed by the **Emperor Huizong**,
Who specially commissioned **Chancellor Zhang Wujin** to further refine and verify.

*The Golden Arrow Rituals and Procedures* **annotate** the **Jade Emperor’s** **Sacred Title** as:
*"The Most High, Opening Heaven, Wielding the Talisman, Ruling the Calendar,
Embodying the **Dao’s** **True Essence**, the **Celestial Sovereign**,
The **Jade Emperor**, the **Heavenly Sovereign**,
Which is the same as the **Title of the Sky** at the **Altar of Sacrifice**."*

Moreover, according to the **Holy Edict**,
In **Heavenly Regard Observatories** across the empire,
**Palaces** are constructed for the **Celestial Sovereign**,
The **Jade Emperor**, the **Heavenly Sovereign**,
To be specially enshrined and revered.
Now, the **Celestial Master**,
**Lord of Lu**,
Has inscribed the **Palace Tablets**,
Which may be followed accordingly.

Furthermore, within the *Daoist Canon*,
The **endless** *Golden Arrow Rituals*,
As well as **Master Cao’s** published *Yellow Arrow Rituals*,
All use the same title.
Only those who understand the **teachings** and **laws**
Can fully grasp their meaning.

In the spring of **Jia Tai Xīyǒu** (1111),
**Elemental Master** **Yuan Su** respectfully records this.

**End of Volume Six of the Daoist Regulations**
**Volume Seven of the Daoist Regulations**

「Western Shu Daoist **Bao An Lu Yuan Su** [1] meticulously verifies and establishes the **Daoist Regulations**,
**Zhu Ling** **True Seclusion** **Xing Zhai Hu Xiang Long** compiles and verifies them.
**Chapter on Settling a Residence**—
On this very day, with reverent words, it is declared:
Only a disciple’s household, which has long adhered to the **Great Dao**,
Diligently tended the incense and offerings,
For self-protection and preservation,
Has no other concerns—
Yet, alas, misfortunes persist.
For the **born of the womb** [2] are of **common origin** [3],
And their excessive veneration often violates the **laws of the Dao**,
Lest the **qi** of **consideration** [4] be delayed.

Upon reflection, it is feared that in the year, month, and day
When the construction of this residence began,
The earth was moved, and the dwelling was established,
The doors and gates were set, and additional rooms were added—
Yet the chosen date was neither auspicious nor propitious,
And the **qi** of the **Earthly King** [5] was offended,
As well as the **Great Year** [6], **Great Yin** [7], **Great Yang** [8], and **Marshal of the Grand Army** [9],
The **Celestial Officials** of that time,
And the **ancient rites** [10] which apply to this present hour—
The moment when a house is built.
This was a mistake in the original text.

Now corrected to the proper time,
Hopefully the confusion is resolved.

For the **Great Expenditure** [11] and **Lesser Expenditure** [12],
The **Twelve Punishments** [13] and **Great Hour**/**Lesser Hour** [14],
The **Twelve Hourly Deities** [15]—
If any infringe upon **Heavenly Prohibitions** or **Earthly Taboos**,
Or if **Heaven’s Void** [16] or **Opening of the Great Dao** [17]
Or the **Opening Day** [18] are altered—
This is incorrect.
The original text mistakenly changed **Void**/**Opening** to **Void-Opening** [19],
Which is not convenient.

Furthermore, it is feared that this house
May be the site where ancient people
Offered sacrifices, made oaths, or held **blood rites** [20],
Or the ruins of hills and ancient tombs;
Or beneath it lies a **hidden soul** [21] or **buried bones** [22],
A restless spirit that lurks unseen;
Or it was once a **temple**, **observatory**, **altar**, or **shrine** [23].
The years stretch on, and the **spirit masters** [24] are not singular—
Lest, through transgression, calamity befall.

Since entering this residence,
The household has faced no ease in dwelling,
Nightmares and ill omens plague their rest,
Strange phenomena arise in all directions,
Wealth is squandered, and misfortunes multiply.
If no disaster occurs,
A few **auspicious nodes** [25] may be omitted,
And the rest follows as written.

All members of the household, high and low,
Are filled with anxiety and prayer,
And seek the **Celestial Master’s** [26] **Scriptures of Settlement** [27]
To clarify the prohibitions,
To secure a peaceful and prosperous residence,
As fully detailed below.

Though unworthy, the disciple humbly submits,
With utmost reverence, a **Red Seal Petition** [28] to the **Celestial Master**,
Praying that the **Divine Qi of the Dao** [29],
The **Marshal Generals of the Five Peaks** [30],
The **Six Jia Deities of Auspicious Power** [31],
And the **Three Marshals** [32] and **Twenty-Four Attendants** [33]
Who guard this household,
As well as the **Thirty-Six Thousand Divine Generals** [34],
Shall take charge for this disciple’s household,
Securing peace and stability in their dwelling,
Eradicating all malevolent and inverted influences,
Water and fire disasters, theft and banditry,
Slanderous tongues and calamitous **qi**,
And every lurking malevolence—
That both public and private affairs may flourish,
And their doors and gates prosper abundantly,
With their wishes fulfilled.

The disciple humbly requests:
That the **Five Marshals of Settlement** [35] be appointed—
Each with **1,200 troops** [36];
The **Marshal of the Grand Army of the Residence** with **1,200 troops**;
The **Marshal of the Residence’s Protection** with **1,200 troops**;
The **Marshal of the Residence’s Preservation** with **1,200 troops**;
The **Marshal of the Residence’s Pacification** with **1,200 troops**.
Together, they shall unite in purpose and strength,
To secure peace in this disciple’s household,
To bless the population with prosperity,
To ensure descendants thrive and flourish,
To suppress all strange phenomena and lurking malevolences,
To silence evil tongues and venomous slander—
And to eradicate every ill omen,
Driving away all malevolent ghosts and demons to distant lands.

May this humble petition be granted
To settle this disciple’s residence:
**Eastern Peace** with the **Azure Dragon** [37],
**Western Peace** with the **White Tiger** [38],
**Southern Peace** with the **Vermilion Bird** [39],
**Northern Peace** with the **Dark Tortoise** [40],
And the **Eight Trigrams for Auspicious Dwelling** [41],
As well as the **Five Directions’ Settlement Marshals** [42].

This disciple’s household has incurred
Countless **prohibitions** and **taboos**,
Yet through the **Scriptures of Settlement**,
They shall receive the **greatest mercy**,
As a sign of **sincere faith** [43].
The **Venerable Sovereign’s** [44] **distinction** is thus proclaimed.

The disciple requests the **Celestial Officials**,
The **Marshal Generals**, and the **Divine Attendants**,
To accept this petition and issue decrees—
That the **qi of construction**,
The **moving of earth** and **building of dwellings**,
The **relocation of homes**,
And all **calamitous expenditures**, **prohibitions**, **transgressions**, and **harmful influences**,
Shall be utterly eliminated,
And that this residence may be secured in peace,
Its inhabitants blessed with prosperity—
Granted by the **Red Seal Petition**.

**Chapter on Settling a Tomb**—
On this very day, with utmost reverence,
The disciple submits their earnest words:

Fortunate indeed is this disciple,
Bound by past karma,
To belong to the **Venerable Sovereign’s** **Great Dao**,
And to all **Celestial Masters** and **Ancestral Deities** [45].
Through the **Three Treasures’** incense and offerings,
They have protected themselves since time immemorial,
And the blessings received are truly cause for celebration.

Yet, the **Celestial Master’s** **precepts** [46]
Are meant to save both living and dead,
To benefit the nation and aid the people,
From the **hidden** to the **manifest** [47].
All who dwell in the realm of **life and death** [48]
Shall be granted safety.

Now, this disciple fears that the **deceased ancestor’s** tomb,
Though still marked by **restraint and misfortune** [49],
Has not yet found peace.

The departed are not meant to suffer,
Yet their **retribution** [50] shall be passed onto future generations—
The tomb becomes a site of **litigation** [51],
A calamity for their descendants.

Thus, they seek the **Celestial Master’s** **Scriptures of Settlement**
For deliverance and salvation.

Unworthy though I am,
I humbly submit a **petition**,
To be delivered to the **Heavenly Treasury** [52].

May the **Venerable Sovereign Laozi** [53],
The **Venerable Ancestral Deity** [54],
The **Celestial Master**,
The **Female Celestial Master** [55],
And the **Five Divine Qi** [56] beneath the **Three Teachers’ Gate** [57],
Attend to this disciple’s submitted words,
Grant them **Heavenly Daoist Qi** [58],
And cover with their **auspicious influence** [59]
This disciple’s household, both living and deceased—
All the **ancestral tombs** of this disciple’s family.

On the day of burial,
Should they transgress **Yin-Yang** [60] or the **Four Seasons**,
Or infringe upon **Heavenly and Earthly Prohibitions**,
And encounter all manner of **punishments**—
Or should **mountains collapse** or **stones fall**,
Or **winds and rains** flood and drench the site,
Or **woodcutters and herdsmen** trample it,
Or **fire and torches** burn it—
If it is a **newly buried tomb** [61],
These items may be omitted.

Should construction begin,
And the earth be pierced or **inspected** [62] across hills and plains,
Lest the **spirits** be unsettled,
Or the **Dragon Deities** [63] abandon their posts;
Or should **water and springs** drift and scatter the bones,
Or the tomb collapse and be filled with earth and stone,
Disturbing the **wandering soul** [64] and causing it to flee in terror—
These matters may be addressed as circumstances dictate.

Should the **burial day or hour**,
Or the **direction of the tomb**,
Encounter any **transgressions** or **clashes**,
And offend both the **living and the dead** [65],
It is not fitting for the **Five Clans** [66],
Nor for the **Four Seasons**—
To fall into **Heaven’s Net** and **Earth’s Web** [67],
Or to be struck by **punishments of the Arcbalds** [68],
With the **Four Killings** [69] unhidden,
And the **Six Deities** [70] not concealed—
Or should they offend **Ferocious Deities** or **Rampant Ghosts**,
Or the **Monthly Killing**/**Daily Killing** [71],
And the **spirit** be seized and detained,
With no recourse for redress;
Or should the **destinies** of their descendants,
Male or female, be incomplete;
Or if the **Eight Killings**/**Six Oppositions** [72],
**Eight Generals**/**Eight Trigrams** [73],
**Six Oppositions + Two Hourly Stems** [74]...»

There are differences—
Or when pressed near ancient temples and ancestral shrines,
Where restless spirits and deities cause disturbance;
Or when close to ancient tombs and great mausoleums,
Where the might of the departed presses in,
And the dark paths of the underworld leave no way to manifest.

As listed above, I humbly beseech the **Heavenly Dao’s** merciful protection,
And petition the presiding deities below,
To resolve and exorcise these calamities,
And to soothe and pacify all unrest.

Or when mountain veins are severed,
Let them be reconnected;
When the **spirit** and **hun** are scattered in terror,
Let them be gathered and restored.
Thus the departed may find peace and prosperity,
And descendants flourish in prosperity,
While lawsuits over tombs are severed,
And the sacred groves thrive—
With malevolent spirits driven away.

I respectfully petition the **Celestial Bureau’s** chief officer and one hundred twenty attendants,
And a scholar well-versed in the **Five Classics** with one hundred twenty attendants,
To oversee the **transmigration and elevation** of the departed **hun** and **po** for **Mr. [Name]’s** family—
For the three **hun** and seven **po** of men,
And the three **hun** and fourteen **po** of women—
To absolve them of their **karmic debts**, **punishments**, and **sins**,
And guide them to the **Hall of Blessings**,
Severing all **karmic entanglements**,
So they may forever enjoy purity and auspiciousness.

I further petition the **Chief of Tomb Stability** and twelve officials,
To oversee the protection of the tombs of the departed **Mr. [Name] and others**,
Ensuring the four directions remain serene,
And the burial grounds forever undisturbed,
For ten thousand years and beyond—
Free from all disturbance.

Should anyone uproot trees, or heap sand, stones, and tiles
To crush bones within the mound;
Or should foxes, weasels, rats, serpents, or creeping roots
Assail the remains;
Or should water veins and springs, stagnant mud, or flowing filth
Soak the bones;
Or should tombs be breached, bones scattered,
With wind and rain preventing rest—
All such afflictions shall be redressed:
The stagnant waters shall be drained,
Serpents and rodents driven off,
Wildfires extinguished,
Bones gathered and bones collected,
Foxes repelled,
And roots and vines severed—
Thus ensuring stability and protection,
Free from harm or resentment,
Lest fear and terror take hold.

The petitioned **Celestial Officers, Generals, and Attendants**,
As per the **Statutes**, shall descend—
To transmigrate the departed,
Stabilize the tombs,
Ensuring the living thrive in health,
The dead rest in peace,
With no calamities arising,
No malevolence stirring,
And dreams untainted by false visions—
Free from sickness and misfortune,
With longevity and prosperity bestowed,
And offspring flourishing in purity and fortune—
Thus demonstrating the efficacy of this petition,
As decreed by the **Most High**.

I, your humble servant, now petition the **Celestial Officers, Generals, and Attendants**,
And submit the **Red Seal of Petition for Transmigration and Tomb Stability**.

**Petition for a Prosperous Lineage**
This very day, I kneel and present my plea:
Your servant, **[Name]**, born of mortal flesh,
By fortune’s grace, now serves the **Great Dao**,
And humbly receives its **Mystic Favor**.

May the **Most High** extend mercy,
And take delight in saving all beings.
My past transgressions are confessed,
And my accumulated sins pardoned.

Your servant fears that **[Name]**, in past and present lives,
Has offended the **Heavenly Worthies**,
Lacked compassion in heart,
And failed in filial piety and loyalty—
Acting publicly for private gain,
Hoarding wealth while others starve,
Burning forests and draining lakes,
Drowning children and aborting life,
Destroying nests and startling hibernating beasts,
Valuing trifles while committing grave sins—
Thus severing the lineage,
Plunging into ever-deepening dread,
With no hope of transmission.
Desperate, I now implore your servant,
To submit the **Red Seal of Atonement, Disaster Warding, and Lineage Preservation**,
So that the **Heavenly Tribunals** may hear.

I humbly pray that the **Most High Lord Lao**, **Most High Elder**, **Celestial Master**, **Female Master**, and the **Five Qi Lords** beneath the **Three Masters’** gate,
May attend to this petition,
And transmit it to the **Celestial Court**.

What is granted is called **"buying with full qi" (全音气上)**,
What is requested is called **"buying with present qi" (乞今)**—
But this is the **Most High’s** descent of **Dao-qi**.

From the **East’s Azure**, **West’s White**, **South’s Vermilion**, **North’s Dark**,
And the **Central Twenty-Five True Ones of Nature**—
The **Heaven-One**, **Earth-Two**, **Heaven-Three**, **Earth-Four**, **Heaven-Five**—
The **Generative Numbers**—
May they descend upon your servant **[Name]’s** body,
Preserving life and extending years,
Sustaining decline and averting calamity,
And banishing the **two hundred ghosts of severed lineage**,
So that the **Source of Blessing** may flow unobstructed,
And **karmic retributions** be severed—
Thus ensuring descendants and progeny,
To perpetuate the line.

I respectfully petition the **Eastern Barbarians, Southern Savages, Western Races, Northern Tribes**, and the **Central Three Qin Lords**,
Each commanding one hundred twenty soldiers,
To assemble and descend—
To absolve **[Name]’s** family of the **billions of ancestral sins**,
The **nine generations and seven ancestors**,
And all **kin and relations**—
Both the **prematurely departed** and the **unexpectedly deceased**—
Severing the **eighty-one karmic entanglements**,
So that life may flourish and descendants never cease.

I further petition the **Southern昌 Life-Registry Officials**, the **Nine-Heaven Destiny Registrars**, the **Great Marshal of Life-Registry**, and the **Northern Dipper Life-Registry Officials**,
Each with their attendants,
To assemble and descend—
To resolve grudges and untie knots,
And expiate the **one thousand six hundred and twenty sins** of past and present lives—
Including **destroying nests and covering eggs**—
So that all may be dissolved,
And evil roots extinguished,
With **Three Realms’ karmic names** severed,
And **heavenly and human ties** dissolved.

Should **[Name]’s** sins be profound,
And the **karmic register** decree lineage extinction,
I further implore the **Most High** to petition the **Supreme Sovereign**—
That the **Jade Emperor** may report to the **Celestial Worthies**,
To broaden the **Most High’s** compassion for life.

I humbly request pardon,
To expand the **Most High’s virtue of saving all beings**.

I further petition the **Ten-Directional Lords of Lineage Preservation and Fetal Protection**,
The **Ten-Directional Gods of Lineage and Fetal Protection**,
The **Great Sage of Longevity**,
The **Six Jia and Six Ding Divine Generals**,
And the **Twelve Attendants of the Jade Maiden**—
Each with ninety million cavalry—
To assemble and descend—
To nurture the **fetal roots** of **[Name]’s** household **[Name]’s wife**,
So that the **Golden Chamber and Jade Hall** may be secured,
And all **demons** repelled—
Those that would harm the fetus as a curse—
Ensuring no severance occurs,
And dreams remain true and untainted—
Lest the **prematurely departed** or **unexpectedly deceased** alter form or shadow,
And harm in visions.

To all malevolent ghosts, do not allow them to lurk and seize upon any opportunity to harm the fetus or cut off pregnancy.

I further petition the **Exhausted and Distressed Lords and Officials** numbering one hundred and twenty, and the **Nine Palaces and Eight Trigrams Divine Soldiers** numbering one hundred and twenty, to assemble and descend, and preside over **[Name]’s** household, opening the **Gate of Birth**, increasing lifespan, sealing the **Gate of Death**, nurturing the fetal roots, ensuring the four seasons remain peaceful, preventing calamities and decline, cutting off death, and flourishing descendants. May water, fire, blades, and armies not dare to encroach—thus securing auspiciousness and eternal gratitude to the Dao, as proof of sincerity. The grace belongs to the **Most High**, as decreed.

**Petition for the Extermination of Malevolent Officials and Soldiers**
Though I, **[Name]**, have long been blessed by fortune, I have devoted myself to the Great Dao, always under its protection, yet my devotions have often faltered, inviting censure.

From of late, I have been plagued by malevolent ghosts and demons, unjustly tormenting me, or even entering my household through my own misdeeds. If further details are desired, they need not be written here.

My life now hangs in peril, with no recourse for aid. I humbly submit this petition to the Celestial Court, seeking relief.

I dare not presume my worthiness, yet I boldly present this plea to the **Celestial Tribunals**. May the **Most High Laozi**, the **Lords and Masters**, the **Celestial Masters**, the **Female Masters**, and the **Five Qi Lords** beneath the **Three Masters’** gate, deign to inspect this humble petition and grant it swift ascent, bestowing **Dao-qi** to cloak **[Name]’s** household in protection.

I further declare that the malevolent ghosts and demons have no legitimate connection to **[Name]’s** family. The ancient sages decreed: *"Ghosts not properly honored shall not be worshipped, lest they bring calamity and harm the innocent."* According to the *Zhengyi Statutes* and the *Female Blue Ghost Edicts*, such malevolent forces must be exterminated to ensure the peace of all households.

I humbly petition for the **One Hundred Twenty Extermination Officials and Soldiers** to govern the **Warehouse of Clarity Palace**; for the **Single Marshal of the Grand Star**, with one hundred twenty soldiers, to govern the **Green Canopy Palace**; and for the **Extermination Talisman Officers** and the **Heavenly Royal Brave Officers**, each commanding three hundred thousand soldiers, to assemble and descend, presiding over **[Name]’s** household. Let them root out and destroy all **guest-death ghosts** and malevolent spirits of unrelated bloodlines who, without proper rites, dare to harass—seizing, beheading, exterminating, and utterly severing them, ensuring absolute distinction and purity.

I further petition for the **Male and Female Ghostly Officials and Soldiers**—those who perished from calamity, foul death, imprisonment, blades, beasts, or fire—each numbering fifty, to oversee the expulsion of external ghosts and unrelated spirits who, though not properly honored, still dare to harass the living. Let them be divided into distinct ranks and households, utterly severed, and forbidden from further intrusion.

Should any dare to defy the Celestial Mandate and again harm **[Name]’s** household, may the rivers flow backward, white stones float, chaff ropes stretch a thousand *zhang*, and horse horns grow six *chi*—yet still they shall find no recourse. If not, may they be utterly cut off from heaven and earth, never to disturb again for ten thousand years.

I further petition the **Five-Directional Judgment Gods**, each with twelve officials and soldiers under their command, to preside over **[Name]’s** household, sealing all **repeated calamities**, yearly, monthly, daily, and hourly connections, ensuring they are utterly cut off. May **[Name]’s** household, when struck by disaster, find relief; when sick, recover; may life and spirit remain secure, malevolent influences crushed, and **true qi** flourish. Let all sufferings and misfortunes be dispelled, and may **[Name]’s** household forever bask in the boundless grace of the Dao. As decreed by the **Most High**.

**Supplication to the Celestial Officials and Soldiers**
I humbly present this **Extermination Talisman for the Destruction of External Malevolent Ghosts and Spirits**, which unjustly harm and seek to sever—now to be annihilated.

This petition, if to be delivered, must first be purified in a sacred space with incense. The **Dao Master** shall establish a boundary, seal the door, and meticulously transcribe it. After verification, it shall be sealed in an envelope with protective seals. At the proper time, retrieve it from the altar for ritual use, without further recitation. Follow the law and submit it in secret, then burn it. Within the text and seals, do not mention this petition’s rituals or informants, lest malevolent ghosts intercept and prevent its ascent.

Beware, beware.
