**Petitioner’s Plea:**
This disciple, by virtue of past karmic ties, has encountered **Daoist transformation**, aligned with the **Divine Sovereign’s will**, and is bound to the **Mysterious Registrar’s ledger**. I have received the **Supreme Dao** and the **Honored Lords’ true teachings**, covered by **Daoist virtue and qi**. Though I bear heavy gratitude, my accumulated sins remain unacknowledged—I am ignorant of sacred rites, often transgressing through greed and error, with offenses deepening daily.

Recently, whether through my own misdeeds or those of others, I have suffered prolonged illness for many days without recovery. I fear that my **seven ancestral and nine primordial sins**, along with the crimes of my past lives, have offended the **Divine**, with guilt piling high and no chance for repentance. Or perhaps my deceased ancestors, bound in the **Nine Springs of the Underworld**, await judgment without absolution, their suffering extending to the living. Or perhaps my own life has been marked by **hidden sins and overt transgressions**, violating prohibitions, accumulating guilt. Or perhaps I have caused **intentional or accidental harm**, leaving unresolved debts and grievances, deepening my punishment, trapping my spirit, and bringing this suffering upon me. Or perhaps it is the **Five Phases’ calamities**, the **Three Destinies’ decline**, the **Lunar Mansion’s influence**, or the **Star of Death’s assault**, with **yearly or monthly taboos** converging to bring this peril, threatening my life daily.

The petitioner, overwhelmed by these afflictions, humbly submits this plea, seeking the **petition’s power** to resolve the disaster and illness.

Unworthy as I am, I dare to offend by kneeling in submission, offering the **vermilion seal**, and presenting this to the **Celestial Tribunals**.

I humbly implore the **Supreme Venerable Lord Laozi**, the **Supreme Honored Lords**, the **Heavenly Masters**, the **Female Masters**, and the **Three Teachers**, to follow the **Five Emperors’ Sacred Left-Right Six Jia Clear Laws and Statutes**. I petition **Jia-Zi King Wénqīng** and the **ten gods of the decan**, along with their one hundred twenty officials and ten thousand soldiers, to descend at the appointed time and act on my behalf. Let them **subdue the deceitful ghosts of the Kan Palace** and **heal the diseased qi** in the **Dan Field’s Three Officials and Lower Element**. With **inner and outer reverence**, may they swiftly annihilate the affliction.

I again humbly petition **Chángshēng Jun** (Lord of Longevity), one with twelve officials, to govern within my body, **calming the liver organ**, ensuring the **liver qi flows freely**, and **rooting out the disease**, annihilating it utterly without trace, **slaying malevolence**. The **years, months, days, and hours** shall be transmitted and relayed accordingly.

I further petition **Jiǎxū Zhǎnzǐ Jiāng**, along with the **ten decan gods and their attendants**, each commanding **one hundred twenty officials and ten thousand soldiers**, to descend in due time and act on my behalf, **harmonizing my family’s hearth god and the taboos of my dwelling**, aiding the **Dao’s propagation and transformation**, capturing and annihilating all malevolent forces.

I again petition **Zhào Gōngzǐ** (Master Zhao), one with twelve officials, and **Lǚ Wēimíng**, one with twelve officials, to **stabilize my inner Dan Field**, **calm the mind and guard the spirit**, **protect the heart organ**, and **awaken true essence**, aligning above with the **Three Celestial Cycles** and below with the **Glory Palace (Gānggōng)**, the **Red Chamber (Chìzǐ)**, and **repelling all external malevolence**. The **years, months, days, and hours** shall be transmitted and relayed accordingly.

I further petition **Jiǎshēn Chē Yuānshēng**, along with the **ten decan gods and their attendants**, each commanding **one hundred twenty officials and ten thousand soldiers**, to descend in due time and act on my behalf, **banishing the ghosts of external reverence**, those of **past generations’ punishments, prayers, and curses**, and those **summoned by litigation and posthumous indictments**, all to be **utterly eradicated**, and my sufferings to be **pacified**.

I again petition **Dù Hǔzhǔ** (Master Tiger), one with thirteen officials, and **Zhǐniàn Jun** (Master of Mindfulness), one with twelve officials, to **harmonize my pulse and qi**, **stabilize and guard the lung organ**, ensuring **spiritual fluids flow freely** and the **Canopy of Glory (Huágài) remains pure**. The **years, months, days, and hours** shall be transmitted and relayed accordingly.

I further petition **Jiǎwǔ Wèi Shàngqīng**, along with the **ten decan gods and their attendants**, each commanding **one hundred twenty officials and ten thousand soldiers**, to descend in due time and act on my behalf, **enacting the Great Yin Official’s talismans**, capturing **internal and external malevolent essences**, **subduing corpse-poisoning sorcery**, and **all qi that violates taboos and prohibitions**, to be **swiftly annihilated**.

I again petition **Chén Zǐpíng**, one with twelve officials, and **Tōngshēn Jun** (Master of the Whole Body), one with twelve officials, to **harmonize my vital source**, **calm the sea of qi**, **guard the kidney organ**, **subdue external malevolence**, ensuring **blood and fluids circulate**, **malevolence is eradicated**, and **true essence strengthens**, aligning above with the **gallbladder**, and below with the **Glory Palace**. All afflictions shall be **healed**, and **divine protection shall be secret and profound**. The **years, months, days, and hours** shall be transmitted and relayed accordingly.

I further petition **Jiǎchén Mèng Fēiqīng**, along with the **ten decan gods and their attendants**, each commanding **one hundred twenty officials and ten thousand soldiers**, to descend in due time and act on my behalf, **capturing and removing** the ghosts of **thirty-six generations past**, including the **departed and those who died prematurely**, those **bound by oaths, prayers, and curses**, those **summoned by litigation and posthumous indictments**, and those **transmitted through living descendants**, all to be **dissolved**, my illnesses **cured**, and my calamities **pacified**.

I again petition **Hé Wénzhāng**, one with twelve officials, and **Zhào Zǐyù**, one with twelve officials, to **guard the Spleen’s Granary (Tàicāng)**, **regulate the spleen qi**, ensuring **the five organs harmonize** and **the hundred passages flow freely**, with **true qi circulating** and **malevolence extinguished**. The **years, months, days, and hours** shall be transmitted and relayed accordingly.

I further petition **Jiǎyín Míng Wénzhāng**, along with the **ten decan gods and their attendants**, each commanding **one hundred twenty officials and ten thousand soldiers**, to descend in due time and act on my behalf, **removing the Five Plagues and a hundred poisons**, **epidemics and pestilences**, **internal and external malevolent forces**, **disease-ghosts of the eight and five directions**, **corpse-ghosts and bandits within my residence**, **metallic and stone implements**, and **all malevolent spirits and demons causing illness**, to be **all exterminated and annihilated**.

I again petition **Mǎ Chāozhǔ** (Master Supervisor), one with twelve officials, and **Jiāng Wēimíng**, one with twelve officials. The **six aforementioned petitions** for the **twelve officials** are all **Heavenly Physicians**, governing within my body the **thirty-six thousand gods**, **one thousand two hundred forms and shadows**, **twelve thousand luminous essences**, the **left three souls and right seven spirits**, the **five organs and six entrails**, the **three hundred sixty bones and joints**, and **all spiritual qi**, ever maintaining **clarity and rectitude**, ensuring **permanent peace**, **healing of afflictions**, and **prolonged life and prosperity**. The **years, months, days, and hours** shall be transmitted and relayed accordingly.

I further petition the **Six Ding玉 Females**, the **Six Jia玉 Females**, the **Six Jia Yin-Yang Orthodox Deities**, **Tiānpéng**, **Tiānnèi**, **Tiāochōng**, **Tiānyīn**, **Tiānbǔ**, **Tiānxīn**, **Tiānyīng**, **Tiānrèn**, and the **Tiānzhù Divine Generals**, to descend immediately and **guard my body**, healing my afflictions, with **a hundred deities offering protection**, ensuring **nourishment and defense circulate**, **true qi flows**, and **longevity is extended**, **permanently preserving virtue and rectitude**.

With reverence, I petition the **Twelve Attendants of the Central Palace** to receive and transmit these talismans, **purifying internally and externally**, **clarifying body and mind**, **harmonizing blood and qi**, **expelling malevolence**, **slaying ghostly bandits**, **restraining spirits and binding souls**, **protecting the Three Palaces**, and **stabilizing the Red Chamber**. Let the **Six Jia generals and officials** each **guard their domains**: **Qīnglóng (Azure Dragon) protects the liver**, **Bái hǔ (White Tiger) guards the lungs**, **Xuánwǔ (Black Tortoise) oversees the kidneys**, and **Zhūquè (Vermilion Bird) governs the heart**.

**Huángtíng Zhēnrén** (True Person of the Yellow Court) shall **harmonize the spleen and clarify the stomach**, ensuring **blood and fluids circulate**, **nourishment and defense flow freely**, **divine medicines take effect**, and **talismans descend in secret**, **warding off afflictions and increasing prosperity and years**.

**Sīmìng Zhēnshén** (True God of Fate) shall **re-examine the records**, **inscribe my name in the Green Ledger**, and **erase it from the Register of the Dead**. **Calamities and blame shall be extinguished**.

The **Heavenly Physicians and their officials**, along with the **Six Jia deities**, shall, on the day of their merit, **report their deeds in the Grand Register**, **securing my survival as proof**, their rewards bestowed by the **Supreme Venerable Lord Laozi**, the **Supreme Honored Lords**, the **Heavenly Masters**, the **Female Masters**, and the **Three Teachers**, who **oversee the Five Qi Lords**, **judge and distinguish**, and **bestow the grace of rebirth**, opening **boundless benevolence**.

**Petition of Humble Submission for Rescue from Calamity and Salvation from Illness**

**The Disciple’s Plea in Filth and Turbulent Qi**

I, the humble disciple [Name], long afflicted by sickness and suffering, now beseech the **Six Jia Officials**, the **True Gods and their attendants**, the **Natural Soldiers**, and the **Heavenly Physicians and their deities** to dispel malevolence and heal my ailments. I humbly submit this **Red Petition for Mercy and Recovery of Illness**.

**The Chapter of Lady Wei of the Southern Prison for Renaming, Re-registering, and Calculating Fate to Rescue from Calamity**
**Master Guangcheng says:** When a person’s year or month of misfortune arrives, when their natal star is exhausted, when their life-decree is severed, and when their annual destiny brings harm, one must recite this **Great Chapter of Emergency Rescue**. Thus, calamities shall be dispelled, and fortune and blessings shall descend. First, the petition must be believed, to manifest its efficacy.

**Offerings:**
- Two silver rings
- One hundred twenty *suànzi* (calculating beads)
- Twelve *chǐ* of green silk fate-thread
- Twelve *dòu* of fortune rice
- One thousand two hundred *wén* of petition money
- Twenty-four *chǐ* of purple *luó* silk for fate

**Ritual Direction:**
The petition shall be submitted in the daytime facing east, at night facing north.

**The Petition’s Text:**

Today, I kneel in reverence and present my plea: Though I, the disciple [Name], am of coarse nature and impure birth, I have been fortunate for countless ages to receive the **Dao**, to be ordained under the **Royal Polarity**, and to preserve my life. Yet, through my own folly, I have acted contrary to the Way, inviting misfortune. This year, my path has been obstructed; sickness has pursued me. I fear the **Nine Calamities** will assail me, the **Three Disasters** will converge, that I shall be ensnared in the **Heavenly Net** and **Earthly Web**, my lifespan shortened, my fate exhausted. Demonic and ghostly forces harass me, and even the **Tai Mountain and Mount Tai** could not summon me to their aid. Without merit, I cannot extricate myself—terror grips me day and night.

Though I am guilty and impure, born of the Dao, I now wholeheartedly surrender to the **Way**, seeking rescue and deliverance. I present this petition in sincerity. I, the humble one, cannot bear this plea further; I now lay it bare in the courtyard, beneath the **Great Void**, before the **Northern Dipper**, prostrating myself to submit this **Great Chapter of Rescue** to the **Celestial Tribunals**.

I humbly implore the **Supreme Venerable Lord Laozi**, the **Supreme Honored Lords**, the **Heavenly Masters**, the **Female Masters**, the **Three Teachers**, and the **Compassionate Father and Holy Mother** to bestow **boundless grace**, to pardon my disciple’s ten thousand deaths, and to grant me deliverance from peril and safety from danger.

I now petition on behalf of my disciple [Name]’s **natal star, annual destiny, birth month, day, and hour officials**, each leading their **officials, functionaries, and messengers**, to carry my disciple’s **annual fate ledger** before the **Jade Emperor**, to report to the **Ministry of Fate**, to distinguish the petition, to halt punishments and executions, to erase the **register of guilt**, and to transform short fate into long. If my disciple’s conduct is perverse and contrary, if their lifespan is exhausted, if they are unrecorded in the **Jade Ledger** or unnamed in the **Left Contract**, if the **Three Elements of Life** are erased from the records, if the **Ministry of Fate** rejects them, and if the **Heavenly Sovereign** does not pardon—then I further petition for **suspended judgment, borrowed fate, renaming, and re-registration**, extending life in three-year cycles.

I also request the summoning of:
- **Five each of the Star-Calculating Lords, Fate-Transforming Lords, and Death-Escape Lords**,
- **One thousand two hundred officials and soldiers**, all convened below.

I further petition the **Lords and Clerks beneath the Great Yin** to join my **internal functionaries and messengers**, to present my case before the **Northern Dipper’s Palace**, to act as my disciple’s advocate, to **redeem the Dead Ledger**, and to **rename and re-register**.

I also petition the **East Hua Palace** for the **Nine Dragon Talismans**, to command the **Twenty-four Prison Clerks and Seven-Twenty Officials of Mount Tai’s Eastern Peak**, to **redefine my disciple’s birth name**, to **erase their death records**, to **mitigate their karmic debts**, and to **restore the Three Souls and Seven Spirits** to their body, preventing their dispersal.

I further request the **Supreme Three Heavenly Jade Maidens—one thousand two hundred in number**—wearing **three-ringed headpieces**, clad in **five-colored black-and-yellow robes**, donning **lion-skin shoes**, holding **雄黄 (realgar) medicine** in their mouths, and **jade nectar** in their hands, exhaling **true qi** to heal my disciple’s body from crown to sole, penetrating **muscle and bone**, harmonizing the **six viscera**, stabilizing the **five organs**, filling the **essence and blood**, banishing all ailments, and ensuring **sound sleep and true awakening**, allowing passage through the **Nine Calamities**.

I also request **one thousand two hundred Heavenly Warrior Clerks** from the **Central Heaven**, to descend into my disciple’s residence, to **capture malevolent spirits and a hundred evils**, to purify the interior and exterior, to establish **divine protection**, so that my disciple’s body may be **strong and healthy**, their **true qi descending**, their **four limbs nourished**, their **five organs at peace**, their **hundred passages regulated**, enabling them to **survive calamity, extend short fate, erase the register of death**, and be inscribed in the **Jade Ledger of Longevity**. All ten thousand sins and myriad offenses shall be **completely pardoned**.

On the day of this grace, I shall **proclaim the Five Precepts of the Supreme Venerable** to my disciple, exhorting them to **abandon vice and cultivate virtue**, to **submit to the teachings**, and to **never repeat their transgressions**, taking today as a new beginning, as proof of sincerity. The grace is thus bestowed by the **Supreme Venerable’s distinction**.

**The Disciple’s Offerings:**
Silver rings, fate-thread, money, rice, and patterned silk—all in sincerity and truth—are now presented to the **Celestial Officials, Lords, Clerks, and Soldiers** in this **Petition for Renaming, Re-registering, Fate-Calculation, and Emergency Rescue from Calamity**.

---
**Petition for Rain**

Today, I arrange my plea and declare: Though I, the humble one, am of dust and insignificance, I have been fortunate to encounter the **Dao’s transformation**, the **mysterious efficacy aiding beings**, and the **true teachings spreading**. I now belong to the **Supreme Dao**, under the **Honored Lords**, nurtured by **Dao-qi**, and have been granted **official rank**. Yet, through my failures in cultivation, I have invited disasters. Within the realm, the **proud sun lingers past its time**, impairing agricultural labor, and famine looms as a grave concern.

I reflect upon the state’s paramount importance: **food is the people’s heaven**. If the harvest fails, upon what shall they depend? I fear that within the **celestial divisions**, the **constellations portend calamity**, and within the **calendar’s calculations**, the **land’s fate is exhausted**. Far and wide, the people are scorched, and officials and commoners are alarmed.

「Furthermore, I fear that my governance and administration may be misaligned with proper measures, that punishments and rewards are ill-timed, and that taxes and levies are excessively burdensome, causing the common folk to suffer grievances and lamentations. The people may perform *sèjiào* (sacrificial rites for disaster relief), so this matter should be curtailed.

Yet, I also fear that the four classes of people are ignorant and do not probe the root causes, lightly despising rice and grains, thus inviting blame and retribution. In self-reflection, I feel as if holding ice and fire in my bosom—though mountains and rivers are beseeched with prayers, there is no response in return. Severing my nails to atone, I must seek mercy from heaven alone.

The *dharma* (true teaching) states: *"When mountains and rivers are beseeched with prayers, and sacrificial animals are made pure, it not only profanes heaven but also offends the gods."* Thus, I merely intend to submit a humble petition to heaven.

I now present my petition to the celestial authorities, kneeling in submission to offer this memorial. May it reach the **Supreme Dao** and be heard by the **Heavenly Tribunals**.

I humbly implore the **Honored Lord Laozi of the Supreme Dao**, the **Honored Lords of the Supreme Dao**, the **Celestial Master**, the **Female Celestial Master**, and the **Five Qi Lords** under the **Three Teachers**, to grant divine attention and fair judgment to this petition of your lowly servant, and to transmit it to the **Celestial Court**, so that the great compassion may flow, and the people be pitied. Command the **Supreme Officials** to distinguish the **Five Phases**, establish the **laws and calendrical calculations**, arrange the **Eight Trigrams**, and mark the **nodes and seasons**, ensuring that **yin and yang** harmonize in their proper order, and that winds and rains come in due time.

I respectfully request the **Nine Seas Northern Míng-Jūn** (darkness/obscurity lord), with an entourage of **one hundred twenty officials**, to oversee the **Heavenly Palace of the River**, commanding the **water-*qi*** of the world, and to invoke the **winds and thunder** to summon clouds and bring rain.

I also request the **Celestial Lord of Rectified *Qi*** (正-*qi*君), with an entourage of **one hundred twenty officials**, to oversee the **Central Heavenly Palace**.

I further request the **One Thousand Two Hundred Jade Ladies of the Sea**, clad in **red robes**, to summon clouds and bring rain.

I request the **Lord of the River’s Truth** (河上真人君), with an entourage of **one hundred twenty officials**, to oversee the **Northern Sea Palace of Great Tài-Shān**, commanding the **rains for all the world’s people**, and to invoke the **winds and thunder** to summon clouds and bring rain.

I request the **Five Lords of the Four Continents and Nine Valleys** (四洲九谷君), with an entourage of **one hundred twenty officials**, to oversee the **Palace of Tài-Shān**.

I request the **Lord of the Nine Rivers and Nine Seas** (九江海玄君), with an entourage of **one hundred twenty officials**, to oversee the **Palace of the Nine Rivers**, and together command the **water-*qi* sources and the descent of winds and rains**.

I also request the **Thirty-Six Lords of the River Spirit and Lord Brǔ’s Sons** (河伯、吕公子), to command the **rains and water**.

I further request the **Thirty-Six Lords of the River Spirit and the Water Emperor’s Attendants** (河伯、使水帝子), to invoke the **winds and thunder** and bring rain.

I request the **Lord Míng of the Celestial Platform** (灵台宫汉明君), with an entourage of **one hundred twenty officials**, to summon the **thunder-*qi* of heaven and earth**.

I request the **Lord of the Lesser Dao-Míng** (小玄冥君), with an entourage of **one hundred twenty officials**, to command the **River Spirit, the Water Emperor, the One Thousand Two Hundred Jade Ladies of the Twelve Streams, the Nine Rivers’ Lord of Peace, subordinate officials, and water-*qi* ghosts and spirits**.

I request the **One Thousand Two Hundred Lords of the Nine Rivers’ Dao-Míng, the Nine Valley Lords of the Tài-Shān Palace, the Nine Valley Lords of the Four Waters, the Nine Marsh Lords of the Yáng-Chéng Palace, and the Jade Ladies of the Lakes**, to come together and descend, aligning with the **Upright City-Huáng** (太社城隍) and the **Plausible and Intelligent** (正直聪明). All divine responses shall work in concert, ascending to fulfill the **Heavenly Mandate**, summoning thunder and lightning, water-*qi* and wind clouds, invoking the **winds and thunder** to bring rain, and subduing the **drought-*qi* demons**. In response to this memorial, they shall be eliminated, allowing the **grains to flourish**, the **hundred plants to thrive**, the **winds and rains to follow their natural order**, and the **year’s harvest to be bountiful**. Thus, the nation shall have **stored provisions**, and the people shall have **sufficient grain**. The officials and soldiers I request, along with the **Wind Teachers and Rain Teachers**, and the **Minor Stars of the Early Agricultural Deities** (零星先农) who have shown diligence and merit, shall ascend to the **Three Heavens** and seek **transferred rewards**, as proof of their efficacy. The favor shall be granted by the **Supreme Dao**, distinguishing and apportioning as described.

I respectfully present the **Celestial Officials and their entourages**, kneeling to offer the **Red Seal of Praying for Clear Skies and Supplicating for Rain**.

---
**Petition for Clear Skies**

I now submit my memorial, but as a lowly and mediocre servant, I belong to the **Supreme Dao** under the guidance of the **Honored Lords**. My mandate is received from the **Heavenly Decree**, and I am entrusted with the **people’s well-being**—the governance of counties and prefectures may be applied accordingly. The people say: *"We are fortunate to dwell under the shelter of Your Benevolence."*

Having long benefited from Your sacred grace, yet failing in my cultivation and duties, I have incurred calamity. Since those days, within the realm, **prolonged rain has been the disaster**, with unceasing downpours. The common folk are in distress, and the **sacred rites of the land** are tarnished by this misfortune.

As the year’s harvest approaches, **rice and grains are the foundation of prosperity**. Agricultural labor having been neglected, **famine must surely follow**. I fear that the **nine earthly divisions** bear calamitous blame, and that the **three celestial luminaries** (sun, moon, and star) have shifted from their proper courses, causing the **laws and calendrical calculations** to misalign with this disaster.

I also fear that my governance may be flawed, that rewards and punishments are unclear, and that the common folk’s sighs of despair may have brought forth these unrelenting rains. The people have already prayed and supplicated, so this matter should be addressed.

I further fear that the common folk are blindly ignorant, neglecting agricultural labor and despising rice and grains, thus inviting **Heaven’s retribution**. Reflecting upon my own shortcomings, I feel as though walking on thin ice—my only hope is to submit this humble memorial with sincerity and seek **Heaven’s mercy** through this petition.

I now kneel to present this memorial, hoping it may reach the **Heavenly Tribunals**. I humbly implore the **Honored Lord Laozi of the Supreme Dao**, the **Honored Lords of the Supreme Dao**, the **Celestial Master**, the **Female Celestial Master**, and the **Five *Qi* Lords** under the **Three Teachers**, to shower Your **mercy upon living beings** and grant Your **benevolence to all creatures**, rescuing those who have fallen into ruin and ensuring the **peace of the people**.

I respectfully request the **Nine Seas Northern Dao-Míng-Jūn** (darkness/obscurity lord), with an entourage of **one hundred twenty officials**, to oversee the **Central Inner Palace** and command the **cessation of the unrelenting rain-*qi****, bringing forth clear skies.

I also request the **Celestial Lord of Rectified *Qi*** (正-*qi*君), with an entourage of **one hundred twenty officials**, to oversee the **Central Heavenly Palace**, commanding the **dispersion of clouds** and the **stillness of rain**, and the **retraction of the yin mists**.

I further request the **One Thousand Two Hundred Jade Ladies of the River**, clad in **white robes**, to ascend to the **Heavenly Tribunals** and pray for the **cessation of the unrelenting rains**, shifting the **wind, thunder, and rain clouds**, and for all the gods to return to their respective stations. Thus, the **winds and rains shall follow their natural order**, the **water calamities shall be dispelled**, the **three celestial phases** (sun, moon, and stars) shall shine brightly, the **four seasons shall proceed in harmony**, agricultural labor shall not be lost, the **harvest shall be plentiful**, and there shall be no fear of **flooding or drowning**. The people’s wish for **life and prosperity** shall be fulfilled, and **original blessings** shall be preserved, as proof of Your efficacy. The favor shall be granted by the **Supreme Dao**, distinguishing and apportioning as described.

I kneel to offer the **Red Seal of Praying for Clear Skies and Eliminating Disasters**.

---
**Petition for Eliminating Disasters and Passing Calamities**

---

Yet a humble disciple born in this mortal world, endowed with past virtuous connections, has received the **True Auspicious Fortune** (*Zhēnxiù*) and reverently heard the **Dao’s Transformations** (*Dàohuà*). But as a mere mortal lost in delusion, I have transgressed the sacred laws—sometimes **contradicting the Saints and defying the True Dao**, sometimes **raising structures or disturbing the earth**, entangled below by the **Five Aggregates** (*wǔyùn*), and above, **obscuring the Three Lights** (*sān guāng*).

I take form from Heaven and Earth, yet fail to grasp their **cyclical revolutions** (*huíxuán*); I am born of Yin and Yang, yet do not comprehend their **natural order and reversals** (*nìshùn*). My actions stray from **Supreme Reason** (*Zhìlǐ*), and thus I dwell in fault. Before I can fully repent and atone, calamities may arise.

Moreover, I fear that in this flowing year and fateful destiny, I may encounter **disasters of cosmic collision** (*liúnián yùnxìan*); or that my **native life-star** (*běnmìng yuánchén*) may meet with **karmic afflictions or malefic influences** (*xīngkè zhī è*).

Heaven’s snares and Earth’s nets—who knows the path to escape? My **lifespan and fortune** (*lùsuàn shòulíng*)—how may I secure the numbers of **prolonged blessing**? Therefore, I humbly turn to the **Great Dao** and devoutly offer obeisance to the **Most Supreme Truth** (*Zhìzhēn*), solemnly preparing the **rites of Daoist faith** (*Fǎxìn zhī yí*) and reverently presenting **modest offerings** (*píngcháo zhī xiàn*).

I petition the officials to intercede on my behalf, though I am unversed in the **mysteries of *qi* and climate** (*qìhòu*). They shall grant my request and, in earnest, dispatch **Five Lifespan Lords** (*Shòusuàn Jūn*), **Five Life-Protectors** (*Bǎomìng Jūn*), **Five Disaster-Dispellers** (*Xiāozāi Jūn*), **Five Calamity-Dissipators** (*Sànhuò Jūn*), **Five Vigor-Sustainers** (*Fúshuāi Jūn*), **Five Affliction-Transcenders** (*Dù’è Jūn*), **Five Net-Solvers** (*Jiěluówǎng Jūn*), and **One Hundred Twenty Attendants** (*Guānjiàng*), to be **united and sent forth swiftly** (*yīhé láixià*).

They shall proceed to the **Celestial Bureau** (*Tiān Cáo*) and **Earthly Registry** (*Dìfǔ*), to the **Ancient Shrines** (*Gǔmiào*) and **Spiritual Altars** (*Língtán*), to the **local deities and administrative officers** (*shèjì jiànglì*), and to the **Department of Life and Death** (*Sīmìng Cáo*), seeking out this disciple’s household—from **beginningless time** (*zì wúshǐ yǐlái*), where sins arise in the heart and deeds, all **recorded offenses** in the **Black Ledger of Evil** (*èbù*), shall be **completely pardoned and erased**.

From **embodied existence** (*zì yǒuxíng yǐlái*), where life is decreed by Heaven and bound by fate, all **destined blessings of longevity and fortune** (*shòulù*) within the **Yellow Talismans of Fixed Allotment** (*Huángqiú*) shall be **extended and fulfilled**.

Should **disasters or afflictions** arise, they shall be **swiftly dispelled and averted**.

「Should **plagues or calamities** (*bìng yīng*) arise, all shall be **dispelled and resolved**. To **transform misfortune into blessing** (*yì huò bài ér zēng fú zhǐ*), and **shift suffering into peace** (*biàn jí kǔ ér zhì kāng níng*), every **obstruction or hindrance** (*zǐwāng*) shall be **completely dissolved**.

I, your humble servant, **devoutly petition** (*chén qíng qí jīngyì*) this to the **Heavenly Department of Life and Death** (*Tiān Cáo*), earnestly beseeching the **Dao/Way** (*Dàdào*) to **bestow compassion**, and the **Supreme Truth** (*Zhìzhēn mìjiàn*) to **inspect in secret**. May it be granted that this disciple’s **recorded offenses** (*zuìjí*) be **severely cut away**, **meritorious deeds** (*shàn gōng*) be **duly inscribed**, the **allotted span of life** (*shòu suàn*) be **prolonged**, and the **fixed blessings of fortune** (*fú lù zhì shù*) be **richly bestowed**.

May **pestilences and epidemics** (*yìlè*) be **banished**, **calamities and afflictions** (*jiěshì zāi yīng*) be **explained away**, and **cessation of movement** (*dòng zhǐ*) be **achieved in tranquility**. May **both public and private affairs** (*gōngsī*) be **protected in auspicious prosperity**, and all undertakings **proceed harmoniously**, with **entry and exit** (*chūrù*) bringing **benefits and ease**.

Next, I humbly pray that **all descendants** (*zǐsūn*) may **equally enjoy blessings and fortune**, that the household be **marked by joyous auspiciousness**, that **no sickness or pestilence** (*jìlè*) may **intrude upon the home**, and that every individual **rely upon the vast benevolence** (*hóng yóu*), generation after generation **enduringly depend upon the shelter of the Dao/Way** (*dào yìn*). May this grace be **uniquely attributed to the Supreme** (*Tàishàng*).

---

**Supreme Chapter for Eradicating Locusts and Plagues, Averting Disasters from Crops**

On this very day, I **bow in reverence** (*qǐshǒu liècí*) and submit these words. By **virtue of past blessings**, I have **received the Dao’s transformation**, early **entered the official ranks**, and **deeply benefited from Heaven’s grace**. Though my **responsibilities are heavy and my abilities light**, I **constantly fear exposure to calamity**. If I do not **personally cultivate strict self-discipline**, how dare I **neglect diligent service**?

Yet I worry that **law enforcement may be unclear** (*zhífǎ bùmíng*), and **disciplinary standards lax** (*jìgāng chǐhuáng*), thereby **contradicting Heaven and Earth’s benevolent intent to nurture life**, and **failing the Emperor’s compassionate care**. The people are not yet **at peace in modest prosperity**, and resources may **fall into disarray**.

Moreover, **the state depends upon its people as its foundation** (*guó yǐ rén wéi běn*), for **when the foundation is firm, the realm is secure**. **People rely upon food as their Heaven** (*rén yǐ shí wéi tiān*), and **when sustenance is abundant, the populace thrives**. Thus, I **prohibit idleness and gaming**, and **ban extravagance and reckless spending**, to **cherish the people’s labor**. I **urge agriculture and sericulture**, and **strive for diligent farming and weaving**, to **cherish the people’s time**.

If **labor is not wasted** and **time is not misused**, while **aligning with Heaven’s seasons** and **enjoying Earth’s bounty**, then **the four quarters shall rejoice in harmony**, and **all lands shall flourish in peace**. The ruler shall **need do nothing above**, and the people shall **take joy below**, for **this is the great foundation of the state and the essential principle of governance**, esteemed since ancient times.

Now, with **the people weakened and the land impoverished**, we **redouble our efforts day and night**, forgetting weariness, and **devote ourselves to cultivation and harvest**. Though the crops **have flourished and grown strong**, and **harvest shall soon arrive**, yet **disasters and calamities persist**, as **locusts and pests** (*mínghuáng*) ravage. The **cries of lamentation and resentment** (*āo’āo bēiyuàn*) rise to **Heaven**.

Truly, it is **our mismanagement and cold-hearted governance** (*zhèngmiù huàliáng*) that **virtue is scarce and talent lacking**. We **knock our hearts in self-reproach**, **regret our errors**, and **pray for Heaven’s mercy**, deeply **remembering the toilers in the fields**, whose **sorrows we have only increased**.

Thus, with **fasting and ritual purification**, we **bow in humility and submit these words**, **returning sincerity with reverence**, and **confessing our past transgressions** (*chànxiè dàoqián*). Your servant, having **observed the fundamental sentiments** (*yuán yuán zhī qíng*), finds **reason to plead**, and **dutifully presents this petition**, praying that the **Nine Heavens** (*Jiǔ Tiān*) may **hear our supplication**.

Humbly, we **beg the Supreme Dao/Way** (*Tàishàng Dàdào*), the **Honored Lords** (*zhūjūn zhàngrén*), the **Three Teachers** (*Sān Shī*), and the **High Officials** (*Shàngguān diǎnzhě*), to **extend compassion and deliverance**, and **not impose punishment**, so that we may **transcend earthly burdens**, **enter the path of the Law**, **assist in the Dao’s transformation of the world**, and **join in the return to the Mysterious Way**.

Yet we, **dwelling among the dust and engaging with the world**, **mixed with the vulgar and the common**, have **no notable achievements** (*gōngyè wèiwén*), and **our sins accumulate**. We fear that **calamities may extend to future generations**, and **our offenses may bring shame to the Three Teachers**. We **personally confess to the Three Officials** (*Sān Guān*), and **daily reflect upon the karmic retribution** (*fēngdāo kǎozhuó*). We dare not **rest in ease**.

With **repentance and fasting**, we **submit these words in earnest prayer**, **returning sincerity with reverence**, and **confessing our past transgressions** (*chànxiè dàoqián*). Your servant, having **observed the fundamental sentiments** (*yuán yuán zhī qíng*), finds **reason to plead**, and **dutifully presents this petition**, praying that the **Nine Heavens** (*Jiǔ Tiān*) may **hear our supplication**.

Humbly, we **beg the Supreme Dao/Way** (*Tàishàng Dàdào*), the **Honored Lords** (*zhūjūn*), and the **众灵** (*zhònglíng*), to **listen to our plea**, **take pity on our sincere hearts**, and, if **granted favor**, to **willingly proclaim this to the Three Officials, Five Emperors, Five Peaks, and all Spirits**.

Humbly, we **beg the Supreme Dao/Way** to **redeem and elevate** us, along with the **Three Teachers and Nine Ancestors**, to **ascend to the Southern Palace**, where **we shall be adorned with official insignia**, **our withered bones transformed into celestial vitality**, and **our hidden consciousness enlightened**, so that we may **receive the Dao’s transformation at the Gate of the Immortal**.

Those **already departed spirits** (*yǐqiān zhī líng*) shall **advance in rank to the Hall of the Red Court**.」

We humbly **inscribe our names** and **engrave them upon** the **Nine Celestial Registers** (*Jīnté gǎobáozàng shénxiān qìjí*) of the **Honored Lords** (*zhūjūn*) and **Immortal Dao/Way** (*shénxiān Dàodào*).

We **solemnly petition** the **Nine Qi Celestial Sovereign** (*Jiǔqì Qīngtiān Qīngdì Tiānjūn*), **Celestial Sovereign of the Azure Waist** (*Qīngyāo Yùnǚ*), and the **Green Dragon Martial Host** (*Qīnglóng bīngmǎ*) of **One Hundred Million Officers and Soldiers** (*jiǔyì wànrén*), along with the **Officials of Jia-Yi** (*Jia-Yi guānjiàng*), to **unify and descend**, entering our bodies and **settling the Liver** (*gānfǔ zhī gōng*).

We **further petition** the **Three Qi Celestial Sovereign** (*Sānyuè Dāntiān Chìqì Tiānjūn*), **Supreme Vermilion Sovereign** (*Tàidān Yùnǚ*), and the **Officials of Bing-Ding** (*Bīng-Dīng guānjiàng*), along with the **Red Dragon Martial Host** (*Chìlóng bīngmǎ*) of **Three Hundred Million Officers and Soldiers** (*sānyì wànrén*), to **unify and descend**, entering our bodies and **settling the Heart** (*xīnfǔ zhī gōng*).

We **further petition** the **One Qi Celestial Sovereign of the Great Yang Emperor’s Mountain** (*Yuányáng Dàdì zhī shān yīqì zhī tiān*), **Celestial Sovereign of the Yellow Emperor** (*Huángdì Tiānjūn*), **Supreme Emperor of the True Person** (*Tàidì Zhēnrén*), **Celestial Sovereign of the Yellow Court** (*Huángtíng Yùnǚ*), **Celestial Sovereign of the Azure Waist** (*Tiāncāng Yùnǚ*), and the **Officials of Wu-Ji** (*Wù-Jǐ guānjiàng*), along with the **Yellow Dragon Martial Host** (*Huánglóng bīngmǎ*) of **Twelve Hundred Million Officers and Soldiers** (*shí'èr yì wànrén*), to **unify and descend**, entering our bodies and **settling the Spleen** (*pífǔ zhī gōng).

We **further petition** the **Seven Qi Celestial Sovereign of the Pure White Sovereign** (*Qīqì Sùtiān Báidì Tiānjūn*), **Supreme Pure Sovereign** (*Tàisù Yùnǚ*), and the **Officials of Geng-Xin** (*Gēng-Xīn guānjiàng*), along with the **White Dragon Martial Host** (*Báilóng bīngmǎ*) of **Seven Hundred Million Officers and Soldiers** (*qīyì wànrén*), to **unify and descend**, entering our bodies and **settling the Lungs** (*fèifǔ zhī gōng).

We **further petition** the **Five Qi Celestial Sovereign of the Mysterious Black Sovereign** (*Wǔqì Xuàntiān Hēidì Tiānjūn*), **Celestial Sovereign of the Night Radiance** (*Yèguāng Yùnǚ*), and the **Officials of Ren-Gui** (*Rén-Gǔi guānjiàng*), along with the **Black Dragon Martial Host** (*Hēilóng bīngmǎ*) of **Five Hundred Million Officers and Soldiers** (*wǔyì wànrén*), to **unify and descend**, entering our bodies and **settling the Kidneys** (*shènfǔ zhī gōng).

We **further petition** the **Three Elements and Nine Departments** (*Sānyuán Jiǔfǔ*), **Five Peaks and Four Rivers** (*Wǔyuè Sìdú*), **Nine Palaces True Persons** (*Jiǔgōng Zhēnrén*), **Immortal Dao/Way Sovereigns** (*shénxiān Yùnǚ*), and the **Martial Hosts of Cavalry** (*bīngmǎ qíchéng*), each with **Nine Hundred Million Officers and Soldiers** (*jiǔyì wànrén*), to **unify and descend**, **distributing themselves within our organs**, **settling our forms**, and **harmonizing the Five Zang and Six Fu** (*wǔzàng liùfǔ*). Within our **Three Elements and Nine Palaces** (*sānyuán jiǔgōng*), **the single body**, they shall **follow and regulate the circulating vital forces** (*yíngwèi*), **uniting the soul and refining the spirit** (*héhún jiǎnpò*), **preserving the spirit and nurturing the essence** (*bǎoshén yǎngjīng*), **gathering the qi and refining the Dao/Way** (*shèqì liànxiān*), **congealing the marrow into the Dao/Way** (*gǔsuǐ níngxiān*), **forming the blood and vessels into truth** (*xuèmài chéngzhēn*), and **donning the Dao’s essence** (*cháofú yuánjīng*), **five-stalked herbs** (*wǔyá zhīyīng*) flourishing, **rinsing the Jade Pool** (*shùmǎn yùchí*), **vital fluids spontaneously arising** (*jīnyè zìshēng*), so that our **bodies may achieve flight** (*shēndé fēixíng*), **transcending the Three Calamities and Eight Difficulties** (*Sānměi Bānàn*), and all **evil influences** (*zhōng'è*). **Thousand perils and myriad poisons** (*qiānxiōng wàndú*) shall **all be dispelled** (*mòbù xiāowáng*), our **enlightened nature** (*huìxìng*) **clearing and bright** (*sūmíng*), **penetrating and comprehending profound truths** (*dòngwù yōulǐ*). The **Honored Lords and Immortals** (*shénxiān*) shall **descend to receive us**, **merging with the Dao’s truth** (*yǔdào hézhēn*), so that we may **neither burden the Three Teachers and Nine Ancestors** (*shàng bùlèi Sānlǎo Jiǔzǔ*), nor **fail to guide the Six Realms and Four Generations** (*xià kědù Liùdào Sìshēng*), all **achieving radiant enlightenment** (*xián dé guāngmíng*), **free from all entanglements** (*jū wú jiéfù*).

Before our **entry into the Dao** (*wèi rùdào*), yet **after our participation in the True** (*jì cāngzhēn*), we have **committed countless offenses and sins** (*qiānqiān wànzuì*), all **begging to be cleansed and dispelled** (*bīngxiè chūdàng*). We **devote ourselves to cultivating the Dao and propagating its teachings** (*xiūzhēn xíngjiào*), **renewing ourselves anew** (*yǐjīn wéixīn*), and **submit our petitions**, **reaching the Celestial Sovereign’s presence** (*biǎoyù Dìqián*). **We humbly pray** that the **Supreme Dao/Way** (*Tàishàng*) may **illuminate and inspect** our case, **universally commanding all spirits** (*pǔguān wànlíng*), **to serve as an example of sincerity** (*wéi wéixiàoxìn*), **the favor of which is boundless** (*ēn wéi Tàishàng yún'yún*).

**Daoist Ritualist** (*Dàoshì*) **begs for Redemption and Liberation from Suffering** (*mièdù bádù túkǔ liànshī shòudù*), **to submit a memorial** (*shàngyán jǐn'àn wénshū*). As a **lowly and unworthy disciple** (*fán yú*), we **have attained the Dao’s scriptures** (*huò cāng jīngfǎ*), **daily renewing ourselves** (*rìniàn zìxīn*), yet **our entanglements remain unresolved** (*jiéfù wèijiě*). **Daring to violate the prohibitions** (*gǎnsuǒ jìnlǜ*), we **disturb the Celestial Sovereign’s purity** (*gānzuò Tiānzhēn*). We **bow in sincere terror** (*chénkǒng chéngkǒu*), **prostrating ourselves repeatedly** (*qǐshǒu dùnshǒu*).

We **humble observe** the **scriptures’ clear prohibitions** (*jīngzhì míngjiè*), **relying on the scriptures’ words** (*kěpíng jīngyán*). **Unless one has prior merit** (*zìfēi xiānshēn*), **accumulated virtue and established deeds** (*lěidé lìgōng*), **or had their name inscribed on the jade tablets** (*míngshū qióngjiǎn*), **they may not presume to access the Dao’s scriptures** (*bùdé wàngjiàn jīngfǎ*).

**Those who have seen** the scriptures **shall all be elevated and liberated** (*xián dé shēngdù*), or **if their merit is insufficient** (*huò gōngdé wèizú*), **their fate shall be annihilation** (*yùn'àn mièdù*). Their **bodies shall pass through the Great Yin** (*shēnjīng Tàiyīn*), **their forms lodging in the Earthly Officials** (*xíngjì dìguān*), **until the appointed karmic conditions are fulfilled** (*yīn yuán qīqì*), when they may **return to their former abodes** (*déhuán gùzhái*). Their **corporeal forms shall receive liberation** (*shīxíng shòudù*), **their spirits ascending** (*húnshén shàngshēng*), **their luminous heads manifesting** (*língshǒu zhāochuí*), **worthy of reverence and veneration** (*chéngwéi xiūfèng*). **We must diligently practice and uphold** (*xiūfèng shénxiān*), yet **daring to follow the benevolent teachings** (*gǎn yuán cíxùn*), we **risk defiling the Celestial Sovereign’s wisdom** (*màodú huángcóng*).

We **solemnly petition** for the **premises of our ancestral temple** (*cǎifù cǎizhōu cǎixiàn*), **our observatory** (*gùnguān*), and **our humble person** (*cǎirén*), **that on the** *certain month, certain day* (*cǎyuè cǎrì*), **at the** *certain hour* (*cǎshí*), **when we humbly perform** *certain person’s* (*cǎirén*) **rites of fasting** (*cǎizhāichén*), we **erect an altar** (*jiù cǎichù jiàn tán*) and **beg to follow the prescribed rituals** (*qǐwèi yīkē xiūfèng*), **conducting the Daoist Ritual of Ascension and Transformation** (*shàngqīng shēnghuà xiāndù qiánshén dào cháng*) for **several days and nights** (*jǐzhòuyè*). From the **hour of** *certain day* (*cǎrì cǎshí*), we **commence the rites** (*qǐshì*), until the **hour of** *certain day* (*cǎrì cǎshí*), **completing the ceremonies and scattering the offerings** (*shèjiào mǎnsàn*). **Our intentions are sincere** (*suǒshēn yìzhě*), yet **we risk offending the Celestial Sovereign’s majesty** (*dānsuǒ Tiānwēi*).

**But a disciple** (*Dàoshì dìzǐ cǎirén*) **humbly submits this memorial** (*jìrì fèngcí dàiwèi wángshī xìngmíng nián cǎsuì yuánmìng cǎ jiāzǐ cǎidì lǐngjí*), **explaining that those who register their names and years** (*yuánmìng nàzhě rú mùmìng rén shǔ Qīngdì*), **such as those born under the Wood element** (*wùmìng rén*), **belong to the Celestial Sovereign of the Blue** (*Qīngtiān*).

**On** *certain month, certain day, certain hour* (*cǎyuè cǎrì cǎshí*), **our departed master** (*wángshī*) **was born**, **receiving their fate from** *certain Celestial Sovereign* (*cǎ Tiān*). **If they were born under the Five Emperors’ Wood element** (*rú Wǔdì zhī shǔ wùmìng rén*), **then they belong to the Blue Celestial Sovereign** (*jiù shì Qīngtiān*).

**During their lifetime**, they **earnestly aspired to the Great Dao** (*zǎo mù Dàdào*), **ascended the altar and wore the Daoist talisman** (*dēng tán pèiqì*), **offering reverence and upholding the Dao**. **Yet their bodies were bound to the lower earth** (*dàn shēnlǚ xiàtǔ*), **tainted by impurities** (*huìzhuó suǒqiān*), **their merit incomplete** (*gōngdé wèibiàn*), **their fate exhausted** (*yùnshù zōngqióng*).

**On** *certain year, certain month, certain day, certain hour* (*cǎnián cǎyuè cǎrì cǎshí*), **they departed due to** *certain illness* (*cǎjì*), **their spirits lodging in the Great Yin** (*shén tuō Tàiyīn*), **their forms residing in the Earthly Officials** (*shīxíng jì dìguān*). **If they have not yet been buried** (*rú wèizàng*), **their remains are now in the Mortuary Palace** (*yún jīn tíngzāng gōng*), awaiting a **favorable day** (*xiū liángrì*), **to be relocated to the ancestral graves** (*qiánhuán gāolǐ*).

**Their merit is still insufficient** (*gōngdé wèibèi*), **preventing them from ascending** (*shàngzú chāoshēng*), **fearing they may be driven and coerced by the Earthly Officials** (*kǒng wéi tǔfǔ suǒjiàn bùxiāng róng'ān*), **their spirits restless and unsettled** (*húnpò fēiyáng*), **their bodies not at peace** (*shīxíng mǐníng*), **disturbing the karmic reckoning** (*yáodòng kǎoduì*), **and being seized by the officials of the underworld** (*zhùdài jiàncún*). **The deceased shall not find rest** (*sǐzhě bù'ān*), **and the living shall face many hardships** (*shēngrén duōnàn*).

**But disciples** (*Dàoshì dìzǐ cǎirén*) **of this humble lineage** (*shēnwèi fǎsì*), **as Heaven-ordained kin** (*yú Tiān shǔqīn*), **grieving the pain of distant loss** (*huái zhuīyuǎn zhī tòng*), **daring to rely on the Dao’s compassionate transformation** (*gǎn yuán Dàdào cíbēi zhī huà*), **and the scriptures’ mercy in guiding the deceased** (*jīngfǎ dùrén zhī ēn*), **we humbly beg** (*xiàng chén qǐ wángshī*) **that our departed master** (*wángshī*) **and those recently deceased** (*xiānwáng jìnshì*), **along with all spirits and consciousness** (*yīqiè húnshí*), **may be granted liberation**.

We **solemnly petition** for the **Supreme Dao/Way** (*Tàishàng Lǎojūn, Tàishàng Zhàngrén, Tiānshī, Nǚshī, Sānlǎo Jiānménxià Wǔqì Jūn*) **to receive our memorial** (*liúshén píngxǐng xiǎocén suǒshàng zhāngshū*), **and to transmit it to the Celestial Sovereign’s presence** (*tōngxíng shàngyù*).

We **beg that the Dao’s qi may descend and flow** (*qǐyì dàoqì xiàliú*), **covering and purifying our recommended departed master** (*fù

If the **threefold wheel of suffering**—the **Five Paths of torment**, the **realms of spirits and ghosts**, the **Six Heavens of Yángmǎng**, and the **Nine Abysses of punishment**—all may be **liberated, delivered, and rescued**.

If the **high Daoist seventh ancestor** of this disciple, **lay and ordained** who have passed, **recently deceased kin**, **former and present lives**, and **those bound by past sins recorded in the Three Officials’ ledgers** and **registered in the Nine Registries**, may the **Ten Directions’ Flying Celestial Officials** all **dissolve their bonds** and **grant them complete release**.

We **petition through this memorial** that the **Three Officials and Nine Registries** in the **Netherworld authorities**, the **realms of spirits and ghosts**, and **all the shadowy prisons** may **record the deceased’s virtuous deeds in life**, **free their spirits**, and **restore them to rebirth**.

We **pray to the Nine-Heaven Sovereigns**, the **Five Emperors and Venerable Deities**, that they **restore their flesh and bones**, **renew their spirits**, **nurture them through the Three Elements**, **shape them with the Nine Qi**, **harmonize their meridians and vessels**, and **infuse them with vital essence**. May those destined to **transform be transformed**, those destined to **be liberated be liberated**, and those destined to **be reborn be reborn**.

May the **deceased’s native mountain**—if of **Wood Command**—be **East Peak Mount Tài**. May the **true and upright spirits** **issue talismans to the Nine Earthly Officials**, each **guarding their domain**, **protecting the corpse**, **as per the盟真科旨**, so that **the body rests in peace**, the **soul remains steadfast**, the **spirit does not scatter**, and after the **memorial’s ascension**, they may **receive pardon**, **quickly attain rebirth**, **ascend to blessed realms**, and **find their tombs and spirit-pivots undisturbed**, free from calamity—**thus proving the efficacy of this plea**. May the **Supreme Dao/Way** **distinguish and grant mercy**.

The **foregoing and following collected memorial texts** are **verified against the Canon’s original**.

The **Celestial Officials** invoked are **all confirmed** according to the *Thousand-Two-Hundred Officials Scripture* **granted by the Supreme Dao/Way**, **each meticulously matched and published**.

It is observed that **recently compiled memorial texts**, such as those for **Wénchāng exorcisms of water and fire**, not only **offend propriety in phrasing** but also **invoke officials based on private speculation**, **fabricated without foundation**. Upon **exhaustive examination of the *Thousand-Two-Hundred Officials Scripture***, these officials **are nowhere recorded**.

For instance, the *Yán Gōng Zhāng* **should omit** such details as **offering jade tablets, painting talismans, erecting altars, or specifying dates from dawn on the *x* day to the *y* hour**—yet these are **redundantly included**. It is **unbecoming** to **alter or omit** from the **established *Thousand-Two-Hundred Officials Scripture***—**lest it become a demonic distortion of the Dao’s teachings**. **Ignorant scribes**, unaware of the **ritual’s weight**, **presume to revise**, **misunderstanding the stakes of ritual mastery**. Moreover, **errors in phrasing and omissions in text** abound.

Those in **supervisory roles** may **reject such works**, risking **condemnation by the Three Officials** and **failure to ascend**. Yet **this transgression against the Dao’s laws is intolerable**. The **uninformed will surely discern it**.

**Recorded in mid-summer, the Year of *xīn-yǒu* (1321), by Retreat Hall Lü Yuansu**, in **conformity with the Dao’s established ordinances, Volume Seven complete, Volume Eight**.

**Verified by the Western Shu Daoist Pǔ’ān Lü Yuansu** and **compiled by Zhūlíng Zhēnxuàn Xìngzhāi Hú Xiānglóng, Master of the Eight Thunders, True Scripture**.

Dare any delay!"*

Bowing in reverence to the Celestial Rites.
The Sun’s luminous brilliance—
Vast and boundless, what thoughts does it hold?
Now I kneel before the Golden One,
Awaiting the Heavenly Hero’s noble form.
The Imperial Daughter of Splendor descends,
Gracing the hall at this hour.
Here, I humbly petition the True Lord of the Sun
To avert my calamitous fate,
Extend my years,
And solemnly present this plea.
All below follows the same."*

**True Form Incantation of the True Lady of the Moon**
*"Gazing upward to the Eight Directions,
Where the Moon nurtures the yin essence.
Within dwells the Supreme Sovereign,
The Lady riding the green palanquin.
Her radiance spans the Two Poles,
Illuminating the Three Pure Ones.
With earnest devotion, I seek the Dao—
Five-colored lights descend to welcome me."*

**True Form Incantation of the True Lord of Wood Star (Jupiter)**
*"The Year Star rides the Wood Virtue,
Turning radiant toward the East.
Heaven’s nourishing dew descends,
His true color shines resplendent.
Singing of flowers, the waves surge grand,
Splashing water, the hall of jade resounds.
Frequent prayers bring natural blessings."*

**True Form Incantation of the True Lord of Fire Star (Mars)**
*"The Mang and Angle Stars—
Dragons and phoenixes, their might commands the Ten Directions.
The crimson blade blazes through five nights,
The vermilion fire flares at three borders.
The incantation’s brilliance aligns with the vital qi,
Swords and spears gleam with martial might.
Demons and comets dare not approach."*

Luminous and vast, the Long Regulator shines.
His peak repels bandits,
His luster dispels armies.
The incantation probes fate’s numbers,
Uniting with the Dao for eternal life."*

Long descending from the Golden Heaven."*

**True Form Incantation of the True Lord of Earth Star (Saturn)**

Hidden lands rise to the Heavy Sky.

The Nine Soils bear radiant light.
Sweet and bitter stones reveal their secrets,
The Taoist and shaman’s calculations soar.
The Celestial Sage bestows dew and rain,
The humble kneel in reverent song."*

**True Form Incantation of the True Lord Luo (Luo Star of the Big Dipper)**
*"The Godhead follows the Dark Way,
Mysterious yet supremely wise.
Dark yet luminous at new and full moons,
Yin virtue eclipses yang’s brilliance.
He guards the Yellow Banner at the Celestial Gate,
Lances and halberds gleam with frost.
With sincere heart, I await abundant blessings,
Bowing to chant the True Scripture."*

**True Form Incantation of the True Lord Ji (Ji Star of the Big Dipper)**
*"Dwelling in darkness, he embodies yin virtue,
His leopard tail steadies the Star Palace.
His wrath shatters mountains,
His might dims the void.
Dragons and serpents spawn monstrous forms,
Sudden transformations plunge all into chaos.
The master’s longevity and fortune,
Averted only through reverence and devotion."*

**True Form Incantation of the True Lord of Purple Qi (Polaris)**

The Jade Chariot ascends the Broad Han,

**True Form Incantation of the True Lady of the Moon’s Comet (Moon’s Luminaries)**

Disasters flow or bless as fate decrees,
Ritual purity pierces the void."*

**The Grand Primordial Transformation of the Supreme Ultimate: The Obscure and Profound Red Text**
*"The Mysterious Master says: The Grand Primordial Transformation,
The divine spirit of the Supreme Ultimate.
The Red Text’s sacred inscription,
The Celestial True One, the Imperial Man—
Descending from the Pure and Clear Hall of the Supreme Victory,
Granting the Great Daoist Law of the Void,
To the Eastern Celestial Chancellor, the Obscure Spirit Official,
Leading the Left Register of the Primordial Birth,
And all the Daoist officials—
The Nine Heavens’ Total Brahman, the Eight Emperors’ Governance of Heaven.
Without the Obscure and Profound Red Text,
One cannot govern the Nine Yangs and illuminate the celestial degrees.
Thus, the Pure and Clear Void’s Celestial Hall,
Embodies the radiant *qi* of the Nine Yangs,
Refining the True and Pure Daoist Essence—
Forming the celestial realm;
The Vermilion Celestial Hall of the Southern Pole,
Embodies the Vermilion Spirit’s Mysterious Sovereign,
Piercing the Yang’s radiance and the True Daoist Essence—
Forming the celestial realm;
The Azure Celestial Hall of the Great Void, the True Ultimate,
Embodies the Broad Spirit’s Supreme Azure,
Ascending the Yang’s Primordial True Essence—
Forming the celestial realm."*

The Jade Celestial Hall of Jade Spirit and Pure Azure Heaven,
Embodies the Jade Spirit’s Pure Azure *qi* of the Primordial Yang’s Perfect Truth—
Forming the celestial realm.

The Great Celestial Hall of the Great Void’s True Essence Heaven,
Embodies the Supreme Spirit’s Mysterious Azure *qi* of the Three Yangs and Nine Truths—
Forming the celestial realm.

The Ling Celestial Hall of Pure Spirit and Radiant Essence Heaven,
Embodies the Pure Spirit’s Radiant Azure *qi* of the Six Yangs and Mysterious Truth—
Forming the celestial realm.

The Purple Celestial Hall of the Profound Spirit’s Supreme Extremity Heaven,
Embodies the Primordial Spirit’s Purple Azure *qi* of the Pure Yang’s Marvelous Truth—
Forming the celestial realm.

The Jing Celestial Hall of Marvelous Spirit and Precious Azure Heaven,
Embodies the Marvelous Spirit’s Precious Azure *qi* of the Yang’s Essence—
Forming the celestial realm.

The Qing Celestial Hall of Jade Radiance’s Limitless Heaven,
Embodies the Qing Spirit’s Jade Radiance *qi* of the Primordial Yang’s Perfect Purity—
Forming the celestial realm.

The Obscure and Profound Red Text transforms into the Primordial Chaos,
The Primordial Chaos transforms into the Pervasive Mysterious Dao,
Governing the Nine Yangs’ Primordial *qi* of the Dao,
Descending to the Nine Causes,
Reaching the Eight Brahman’s True Speech—
All this is the transformation of the Obscure and Profound Red Text.

Therefore, within the Great Dan Field,
Lies the Imperial Palace of the Ruanli City, the World of the Abandoned Sage,
Ruled by the Brahman Precious Spirit and the Red Sovereign.
Within it are the Vermilion Ling Court,
The Flowing Fire Hall,
The Fire-Flame Palace,
The Red Clarity Lodge,
The Dan Hill Fire Pool—
Where the Primordial Essence of the Celestial Venerable refines the True Daoist Text.

The Brahman also lies in the Heavenly Middle,
With the two True Ones above and below.
Those who cannot attain this,
I now grant you this True Daoist Text,
The Primordial Chaos Brahman Essence Diagram,
To be kept in your possession.
From now on, the Six Heavens—*Yùnhēng*, *Rénchén*, *Hédù*, *Yìngzǐ*, *Qīngzǐ*, *Pínghuà*, *Zìrán*, *Fūlù*—
Their secret and marvelous talismans and inscriptions
Shall all be beyond measure.

**The Eight Banners of the Eight Registers (placed on the lower level’s edges):**
- **Zhèn (Thunder) Palace:** Azure Banner with Black Register—*Qi* of the Zhèn Palace’s Mysterious Azure.
- **Xùn (Wind) Palace:** Yellow Banner with Black Register—*Qi* of the Xùn Palace’s Brahman Conduct.
- **Wǔ (Fire) Palace:** Red Banner with White Register—*Qi* of the Lì Palace’s Mysterious Yang.
- **Kūn (Earth) Palace:** Yellow Banner with Black Register—*Qi* of the Kūn Palace’s Brahman Yang.
- **Dùi (Lake) Palace:** White Banner with Azure Register—*Qi* of the Dùi Palace’s Lesser Yin.
- **Gǎn (Mountain) Palace:** Black Banner with Yellow Register—*Qi* of the Gǎn Palace’s Brahman Conduct.
- **Shēn (Metal) Palace:** Black Banner with White Register—*Qi* of the Shēn Palace’s Pervasive Mysterious Golden Threshold.
- **Kān (Water) Palace:** Black Banner with Red Register—*Qi* of the Kān Palace’s Mysterious Yin.

**The Four Gates (placed at the four corners of the middle altar, using eight long registers):**
- **Mǎo (Wood) Direction:** Azure Banner with Red Register—The Gate of Pure Azure Primordial Yang.
- **Chén (Wood-South) Direction:** White Banner with Yellow Register—The Gate of the Yang’s Primordial Birth.
- **Wèi (Earth) Direction:** Yellow Banner with Red Register—The Gate of the Nine Spirits’ Brahman Truth.
- **Shēn (Earth-South) Direction:** Yellow Banner with Red Register—The Gate of the Mysterious Yang’s Supreme Radiance.
- **Yǒu (Metal) Direction:** Black Banner with White Register—The Gate of the Pervasive Yin’s Golden Threshold.
- **Xū (Metal-North) Direction:** White Banner with Yellow Register—The Gate of the Nine Immortals’ Brahman Conduct.
- **Hài (Water) Direction:** Azure Banner with Black Register—The Gate of the Great Luo’s Flying Brahman.
- **Zǐ (Water) Direction:** Azure Banner with Black Register—The Gate of the Yin’s Broad Spirit.

**The Ten Banners with Twenty-Eight Registers (placed at the four edges of the inner altar):**
The Three Levels’ Gate Supports—twenty-four wooden plaques,
Painted with flying immortals and *qi* clouds above and below,
Striving for utmost precision and craftsmanship.
Beyond the Three Levels, erect flower pillars,
Three *chǐ* in height, and rub them with a five-hundred-*fēn* azure banner.
This is called the Pure Guardian, the Barrier to the Profane.

Below the altar’s lower level,
Open the Heavenly Gate, Earthly Portal,
Day Gate, and Moon Gate.
Above the lower level, install the Ten-Directional Incense Altars.
The Three Levels adjust to the altar’s width and breadth,
Setting up mats and cushions for offerings.
The Celestial Master Zhang Wànfú said:
*"In my past travels through Jiang and Hàn,
Every Daoist temple and observatory
Built earthen altars and wooden structures,
Established registers and banners,
All following the prescribed method.
The registers were carved from wood and painted with lacquer,
Installed with lotus flowers and grass,
And adorned with fire pearls above.
The banner inscriptions
Were borne aloft by cloud dragons and phoenixes,
Or decorated with golden lotus flowers in bronze or copper.
When constructing altars for rites,
Arranging and deploying them as law,
After the ritual’s completion, they were scattered—
Yet stored in great lacquered boxes,
Preserving the talismans and ritual procedures."*

The Three Officials’ Tents are placed on the altar’s east,
The Five Teachers’ Stands on the altar’s west,
Each erected with proper tents and canopies.
Prepare round images and altars for offerings,
As per the prescribed rites.
The Three Officials oversee the Three Primordial Registers of Examination,
Verifying and recording the merit of the fast.
The Five Teachers serve as the primary masters of ritual initiation,
Leading those who store and reflect on the Dao—
Both should be properly positioned on the altar’s left and right.

I observe the altar diagrams of the Zhang and Dù masters,
Which only depict the Three Levels’ altar rites,
Lacking any halls or pavilions.
The prescribed ritual for placing images
Is to install the Three Venerables on the upper level,
And set the Three Officials’ and Five Teachers’ tents
On the altar’s left and right—
Just as in the court’s *Yuánqiū* (Round Mound) rites.
This alone reveals the ancient intent.

The Nine Ancestors’ Positions are to the south of the altar,
To elevate and purify the Nine Profound Realms,
And to cleanse the Mysterious Ancestor—
A seat should be set, facing the altar.

The Earthly Deities’ Positions are in the southwest,
To summon and invoke their attendance,
And to transmit the Mysterious Dao above—
When constructing a ritual altar,
The Earthly Deities are paramount—
A seat should also be set, facing the altar.

**The Supreme Summoning of the True Spirit Talisman:**
Right side, green paper, red script,
As long as the Three Sovereigns’ Text.

The vertical alignment of the upper and lower axes is applied within the altar.

The *Xuánzhōng Jiānzhāi Sānshī Wèi* talisman—all non-*Tiānzhuàn* (Celestial Script) inscriptions, mere human contrivances—need not be applied.

The altar diagram: to the right, the rites of the *Zhang* and *Du* Masters are taken as precedents, verified and compiled for reference. Those who refine their practice will find value therein.

**The *Ānshè Guishén* (Returning the Spirit to Its Dwelling) Talisman**
East, South, West, North, Central
*Qiān* Palace Deity, *Kǎn* Palace Deity, *Gèn* Palace Deity, *Zhèn* Palace Deity, *Xùn* Palace Deity, *Lí* Palace Deity, *Kūn* Palace Deity, *Duì* Palace Deity
Hall, Gate, Gate, Gate, Gate, Gate
Well, Main Gate, Central Gate, Rear Gate
*Ānshè* (Returning the Spirit), Kitchen, Kitchen
Two talismans to the right, inscribed on green paper with red script, to be presented as per the ritual register.

Heaven’s Sentence Weaves the Net.

**The Central Ancestral *Qi*’s Jade Calendar’s Precious Scripture**
*Zhèngyīn*

True Yang Opens Transformation,
The Dharmic *Qi* Flows Unobstructed,
The Golden Gate Lies Above,
The Jade Treasury Resides to the East.
The Five Patterns Congest,
The Nine Spaces Radiate Brilliance,
The Marvelous *Qi* Naturally Forms,
Its Depths Defy Exhaustion.
The Three Spirits Converge in Unity,
Ten Thousand Saints Take Root Here,
Examining Conduct and Learning,
Marking the True Merit.
With Spirit in Accord,
And the Dao in Harmony,
Stabilizing Life’s Scrolls,
For a Hundred Kalpas Without End.

After cultivation and veneration, the following words align with the Precious Hall.
If the method is unclear, the order lost,
One falls into the Realm of Punishment.*

Now presenting the Jade Registrar’s True Talisman,
Beseeching for the Dao-practitioner [Name] of this household,
Who now wishes to change their recorded name—
Uncertain if this entry is proper,
And how the day should be chosen.
Severing transgressions, all granted absolution.

That future descendants may eternally preserve the unbroken line,
And serve the Void Emperor,
All in accord with the Primordial Mystery,
As the Green Sovereign’s Jade Registrar’s Command decrees.

High Functionary, Half-Name [Surname] [Given Name], Declared.

**First Invocation Document of the Yellow Arrow Ritual for Summoning Celestial Deities** (黄箓罗天第一度召请神状 第一状)

**Second Invocation Document of the Yellow Arrow Ritual for Summoning Celestial Deities** (黄箓罗天第二度召请神状 第二状)

Within the **three invocations**, all include the deities of the **Sichuan sovereigns and ministers**, while other prefectures and kingdoms may add or omit local mountain and ancestral spirits according to their veneration.

**First Register:**
The **Supreme Clarity** (太皡) **Fuqi** (伏牺) **Lady**, **Nüwa**, the **Flame Emperor** and **Divine Farmer** (炎帝神农氏), **Suiren** (燧人氏), **Emperor Yao**, **Emperor Shun**, **King Yu of Xia**, **King Tang of Shang**, **King Wu of Shang**, **Hou Ji**, Shun’s ministers, the **ancestors of Zhou**—**King Wen of Zhou**, **King Wu of Zhou**, **Emperor Gaozu of Han**, **Emperor Xiaowen of Han**, **Emperor Guangwu of Han**, **Emperor Gaozu of Tang**, **Emperor Taizong of Tang**, **King of Shu** (蜀賨王), **Duke Ling of Shu** (蜀望帝), **King Yufu of Shu** (蜀鱼凫王), and **Emperor Zhao Lie of Shu** (蜀昭烈皇帝).

**Second Register:**
**Xī Zhōng** (羲仲), **Hé Zhōng** (和仲), **Xī Shū** (羲叔), **Hé Shū** (和叔), **Gāoyáo**, Yu’s ministers—**Āhéng** (殷阿衡), **Yī Yǐn** (伊尹), **Fù Yuè** (傅说) of Shang, **Tai Gong of Qi**, **Duke Wen of Lu** (鲁周文宪王), **Zhōu Gōng** (周公), **Yào Zhāo Gōng** (燕召公), **Duke Wén of Zhèn** (酇文绛侯), **Xiāo Xiànggōng** (萧相国), **Píngyáng Yì Hóu** (平阳懿侯) **Cáo Xiànggōng** (曹相国), **Líú Hòu** (留侯), **King Hàn Xìn of Huái Yīn** (淮阴侯韩王信), **Fányáng Fán Hóu Huò** (舞阳樊侯哙), **Wén Xù Lú Jiāng Bó** (文翕庐江伯), and all below who rendered merit to Shu.

**Third Register:**
Deities of the **Sacrificial Canon**—**Guāng Yòu Yīng Huì Wáng** (广佑英惠王), **Zhāo Líng Guāng Huì Wáng** (昭灵广惠王), **Yīng Liè Zhāo Huì Xiǎn Wēi Jì Wáng** (英烈昭惠显威济王), **Yīng Xiǎn Wǔ Liè Zhōng Yòu Guāng Jì Wáng** (英显武烈忠佑广济王), **Guāng Lì Dà Wáng** (广利大王), **Dōng Yuè Fú Yìng Bǐng Líng Jūn** (东岳孚应炳灵君), **Yì Shùn Yīng Jì Wēi Wǔ Hóu** (翊顺英济威武侯), **Jīn Mǎ Líng Guāng Hóu** (金马灵光侯), **Líng Gé Huì Yìng Fēng Zé Wáng** (灵格惠应丰泽王), **Yòu Dé Zhù Shùn Líng Jì Zhāo Liè Wáng** (佑德助顺灵济昭烈王), **Fú Yòu Wáng** (孚佑王), **Wēi Jì Hóu** (威济侯), **Nán Kāng Jùn Wáng** (南康郡王), **Shēng Lù Bǎo Shòu Hóu** (生禄保寿侯), **Cí Mǔ Shàn Yìng Fū Rén** (慈姥善应夫人).

Should there be deities enshrined within the realm or worthy of veneration, they may be added. However, **licentious rites** or those not sanctioned by the **Sacrificial Canon** must not be included.
